Czech President Explains Foreign Policy 33

Prague, Czech Republic President Beneš delivered a radio address for Christmas, recounting the international situation and Czech foreign policy over the past year. He said that in 1936, the situation of mutual confrontation between fascist countries, communist countries, and democratic countries became increasingly acute. Although the Czech Republic has not abandoned its belief in upholding the League of Nations, on the other hand, it has tried to use other forces to make up for the shortcomings of the League of Nations. For example, the alliance treaty between the Czech Republic and France and the Little Entente countries, the mutual assistance pact between the Czech Republic and Russia, and the friendly relations between the Czech Republic and the United Kingdom and the Balkan Entente countries are all intended to strengthen the forces of peace. Mentioning France, Beneš said that France has sufficient reason to feel worried about its security. Mentioning Germany, he said that the European peace plan put forward by Chancellor Hitler on March 29 of this year should be seriously considered. Finally, Beneš added that the Czech army has been greatly strengthened in 1936, and fortifications have been added to all borders. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Anglo-Italian Agreement; Differences of Opinion Still Exist; Unlikely to Be Established This Year 34

Japan Proposes Negotiations on Pacific Issues; U.S. Expresses Agreement, but Insists All Related Nations Should Participate; Japan Informs Britain, Acknowledges Retention of Old Ships, and Notifies of Non-Destruction of Over-Aged Submarines 35

(Washington) Reports indicate Japan intends to negotiate Pacific issues with the United States. It is understood that the matter originates from the question of maintaining the status quo regarding fortifications and naval bases on Pacific islands (as stipulated in Article XIX of the Washington Naval Treaty). Britain had previously, in September, communicated to both the U.S. and Japan, advocating for negotiations to renew said article. However, neither the U.S. nor Japan offered a formal response. Until recently, Japan began advocating for negotiations with the U.S. U.S. diplomatic circles seem to generally support this proposal, but believe that such negotiations should not be limited to the U.S. and Japan. All signatories of the Nine-Power Treaty, as well as the Soviet Union, should be included, according to a Havas dispatch on the 24th.

(London) Rumors suggest that Japanese Foreign Minister Arita is about to issue a statement supporting joint cooperation between Japan, the U.S., and Southern nations to avoid an arms race in the Pacific. Observers here attach great importance to this rumor and express satisfaction, believing that if this statement is confirmed, it will bring about significant changes to the situation created by Japan's withdrawal from the London Naval Conference. In particular, all relevant countries should be included in any negotiations regarding Pacific issues, with Britain being one of those countries, according to a Havas dispatch on the 24th.

(London) The British government formally notified the U.S. and Japan a few days ago that it intends to invoke Article XXI of the London Naval Treaty, the "escalator clause," to retain five cruisers that have reached their service age. The Japanese Embassy in London formally notified the Foreign Office this afternoon that the Japanese government has also decided to invoke the above-mentioned escalator clause to retain 11,000 tons of submarines that have reached their service age and not destroy them, according to a Havas news agency dispatch on the 24th.

(Tokyo) According to a telegram sent by Ambassador Yoshida in Britain to the Foreign Ministry on the 24th, the British government formally informed Ambassador Yoshida on the 22nd that Britain would invoke the escalator clause of Article XXI of the London Treaty to retain and refit five Class B cruisers exceeding their age, in order to strengthen air defense facilities. Therefore, Foreign Minister Arita, based on the British government's previous inquiry into Japan's intentions, to which he had given an informal response at the time, instructed Ambassador Yoshida to formally reply to Britain immediately, expressing no objection. He also telegraphed Ambassador Saito in the U.S. to make a similar notification to the U.S. government. Meanwhile, Japan, having broken away from all arms limitation treaties from January next year, will regain freedom to build ships. Prematurely abandoning ships exceeding their age and rebuilding them would only increase the burden on the people and defeat the spirit of arms reduction. Therefore, from this perspective, it acknowledges Britain's proposal, according to a Domei News Agency dispatch on the 25th.

(Tokyo) U.S. Ambassador to Japan Grew visited Foreign Minister Arita at the Foreign Ministry on the 24th to communicate the U.S. government's opinion on the issue of cruiser retention. He stated that the U.S. intends to acknowledge the escalator clause automatically proposed by the British government. According to this provision, the U.S. can retain 10% of the total tonnage of destroyers, or 19,000 tons. After the U.S. Ambassador conveyed this information, he inquired about the Japanese government's opinion. The Foreign Minister replied that the Japanese government would instruct its ambassadors in Britain and the U.S. to report their opinions to the governments of their respective host countries. After the two discussed this issue, they also exchanged views on the China issue, according to a Domei dispatch on the 25th.

Trade Issues: Australia and Japan Reach Compromise 36

(Tokyo) The outcome of the negotiations between Japan and Australia is a compromise agreement, the main points of which are as follows:

(1) Japan will import 800,000 bales of wool every year and a half, while exporting 153.7 million square yards of textiles during the same period. (2) Regarding tariff issues, the tariff rates of May 23 will be abolished, and the increase in tariffs will be limited to 5% to 10% for cotton cloth and 5% to 15% for rayon.

The government will consult with the Tariff Investigation Committee on the 26th before holding a cabinet meeting to decide on the cancellation of the Trade Protection Act launched against Australia, according to a Domei dispatch on the 25th.

Britain Organizes New Company to Promote Trade; British Capital, Government Support 37

(London) Powerful figures here are organizing a company to facilitate commerce between Britain's dominions and colonies, and to assist European nations with exchange restrictions that are reducing their normal trade. The main purpose is to barter goods with Germany. The company is purely British capital, and the British government has no objection. The governments of the dominions have endorsed it, and the German government has also agreed to provide certain conveniences and special benefits. The company also hopes to trade with Turkey, Romania, Bulgaria, and Yugoslavia, selling them grains, fats, oils, leather, flax, and rubber. In the event of war, deliveries to belligerent countries will naturally be suspended. According to company officials, trade within the British Empire is expected to increase, because countries like the U.S. and Japan currently only sell goods to British dominions without buying from them. Under the company's new plan, buying and selling must be balanced, according to a Reuters dispatch on the 25th.

The Discovery of the New World Was Not by Columbus, but by a Norse Viking; Research by German Historian 51

Domei Special Dispatch. Columbus discovered the American continent, a very well-known fact. No one denies this. However, Germany recently denied this claim, saying that the first discoverer of the American continent was a Norse Viking. Columbus only stole this pirate's map and made it happen. This claim was made by German historian Dr. Lang English. The doctor mentioned this in his recently published pamphlet, saying: "The world calls Columbus the discoverer of the American continent, which is actually a deception. At that time, there were Norse Vikings, with many followers, who made a living by robbing ships in the Pacific. After looting, they sailed far away to avoid the eyes and ears of the authorities. They happened to discover the American continent and made a map. Over time, this map was transferred to the hands of the Roman Pope's office. When the Pope examined this map, he asked Columbus for help. Columbus stole it and spent day and night recreating a map for his own navigation use. This is actually the basis for his success. It is also unbelievable that the world says Columbus was an Italian, born in Geneva. In fact, Columbus was a mixed-race person of Spanish and Jewish descent," (December 25).

Tianjin Public Security Bureau Dismantles Fake Recruitment Agency, Mastermind Zhang Xueqian on the Run, 14 Accomplices Arrested 52

Tianjin Correspondence: Zhang Xueqian, formerly a section chief of the Beiping Military Branch and a councilor of the 51st Army, a relative of Zhang Xueliang, had been living in Tianjin for nearly half a year since his retirement. Recently, he established a fake recruitment agency in the National Hotel in the French Concession of Tianjin and also set up a fake military headquarters in Hebei's Sanjing Road and Hedong's Fuxing Village. He secretly ordered his accomplices to recruit troops, and the name of his agency was "Commander-in-Chief's Office of the Northeast Army of the National Revolutionary Army." Zhang appointed himself as commander-in-chief and appointed fake division commanders such as Wang Tingxiang, Liu Bichen, and Ma Wu, with appointment letters issued up to number 762. There was also a fake commander-in-chief, Liu Yanbin, who specialized in activities in the war zone. It is reported that the majority of those recruited were scattered soldiers and vagrants from various parts of eastern Tianjin and along the Great Wall, and many bandits from Fengrun and Luanzhou were also absorbed. The figures are as follows: (1) Li Jiasan from Fengrun, with 1,600 men and 60% armed with guns; (2) Wu Xiangsan from Yutian, with 2,200 men and 70% armed with guns; (3) Chen Guobao from Luanxian, with 1,300 men and 50% armed with guns; (4) Zuo Fenglou from Guye, with 3,500 men and 60% armed with guns; (5) Li Shaoting from Changli, with 2,500 men and 50% armed with guns; (6) Xiao Meisheng from Qian'an, with 700 men and 50% armed with guns; (7) Caoshangfei from Funing, with 2,300 men and 70% armed with guns; (8) Liu Yuanhua from Zunhua, with 600 men and 50% armed with guns; (9) Huang Tianba from Linyu, with 280 men and 80% armed with guns; (10) Ma Wu from Leting, with 2,000 men and 80% armed with guns; (11) Ren Cheng from Qinhuangdao, with 3,600 men and 70% armed with guns. The total number of these fake troops is estimated to be around 40,000. However, it is unknown whether the reported figures were inflated for the purpose of extorting money. Zhang Xueqian's plan, as announced to the fake division and brigade commanders, was to use eastern Hebei as a base and then advance towards outside the pass, with a reward of 15,000 yuan for each county occupied. After the troops were recruited and counted, each person would be given an activity fee of five yuan. The Tianjin authorities had a slight inkling of this matter last week and had planned to arrest him, but because Zhang was a graduate of the Japanese Army Officer School and had many classmates in Tianjin, they asked people to intercede for him. The authorities had slowed down their intention to arrest him, but in recent days, they realized that his actions were not simple. Mayor Zhang Zizhong secretly ordered Public Security Bureau Chief Li Wentian to quickly arrest him to avoid harming the local area. At 5:00 PM on the 23rd, Wang Baoyuan, the leader of the Second Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, together with Zhao Chuntian, the director of the Seventh Precinct of the Fifth Sub-bureau, surrounded the fake military headquarters in Hedong's Fuxing Village and arrested Xu Yeqin, Cao Guirong, Li Yongshun, Liu Hanqing, Zhao Deyou, Li Kaiting, Yue Guangqi, Yao Zhenlin, Song Xingrui, Yu Guoqing, Yu Jintao, Li Jinduo, Xu Yonghe, and Zhang Yonglin, a total of fourteen people, as well as Xu's wife and Yao's wife, two people. They found a fake seal engraved with the words "Certain Army, Certain Division of the Fourth Group Army of the National Army," as well as two fake appointment letters, one issued by Wang Tingxiang, the fake commander of the First Division of the Third Army of the Fourth Group Army of the fake National Army, to Xu Yeqin and Cao Guirong. Xu's appointment letter was as the head of the division's martial arts team, and Cao's appointment letter was as the head of the First Regiment of the First Brigade of the division. In addition, there was a roster of the names, numbers of firearms, and locations of the various fake troops in the war zone reported by the fake commander-in-chief Liu Yanbin. The group of offenders was sent to the Public Security Bureau on the morning of the 24th, and the search for their accomplices is still underway. Zhang Xueqian himself is hiding in Ma Doctor's Hospital in the French Concession, using illness as a pretext to avoid leaving the hospital. Although the Public Security Bureau wants to arrest him, they cannot do so. The fake division commander Ma Wu was sent to Baoding to carry out activities and returned to Beiping the day before yesterday. A fake office has also been set up on West Chang'an Street in Beiping. The Tianjin authorities telegraphed the Beiping Public Security Bureau on the 24th to search and arrest him. (24th)

Japanese Ruffians and Traitors Active in Chaozhou, Military and Political Authorities Pay Attention to Prevention, Wang Jianmin Executed by Firing Squad After Arrest 53

Shantou Correspondence: The Chaozhou and Shantou area, bordering the sea and adjacent to Fujian Province, has seen Japanese ruffians frequently engaging in various activities, causing countless international disputes. According to accurate and detailed information, no less than 2,000 Japanese ruffians and traitors have infiltrated the interior of Chaozhou and Shantou. They do not fulfill household registration procedures, carry weapons without authorization, escort smuggled goods, or act as peddlers in the interior, spying on military intelligence and national defense deployments, photographing terrain, colluding with hooligans, and secretly forming societies. In Shantou City and Chaoyang City, people with foreign accents are often found inquiring about local security conditions from shops, but merchants uniformly refuse to answer. The Administrative Commissioner's Office believes that the ruffians have ulterior motives and must be strictly prevented. It has telegraphed the mayors and magistrates of various counties, requiring that if anyone rents a house in urban or rural shops and homes, the owners and co-residents should be required to fill in their nationality, name, occupation, number of residents, and place of origin, and report to the local government, police station, or autonomous public office, obtain a shop guarantee, and complete the procedures before being allowed to move in. If anyone falsely claims to be Chinese and moves in or engages in business, the Public Security Bureau should refuse to issue a license. If any civilians deliberately violate this rule, they will be severely punished once discovered or reported, in order to maintain security. Military police in various counties have tightened security in recent days, checking passing boats and vehicles, and armed sentries are stationed at key transportation points. After nightfall, anyone without a lantern is not allowed to pass. Hotels, inns, and public places are subject to particularly strict inspections to prevent the disruption of traitors. A certain Gao, the leader of the ruffians, used to summon intelligence personnel from various places to Shantou every Saturday and Sunday for two hours of training, guiding their central work. Those who attended the training always walked there on time, without taking cars, nodding on the road, talking, or traveling in groups of three. Since the Xi'an Incident, there has been a meeting almost every other day. Around 7:00 AM in the morning, they would leave one after another, each carrying a floral cloth towel, containing cameras and other items, and go to Chenghai, Chao'an, Chaoyang, and other inland areas (places that can be reached and returned from in one day). Because they either falsely claim to be relatives, are recruited as sons-in-law by poor women, or become friends with party leaders and local bullies, and live in the study rooms or residences of important people in the countryside, doing certain work, their actions are all outside the cordon. For example, Wang Jianmin, the secretary of the Chenghai Party Committee, the former provincial senator, controlled the party departments and autonomous organizations at all levels in the county, and usually oppressed the people, used the party for personal gain, secretly colluding with ruffians, packing and transporting smuggled goods, and willingly acted as a traitor. Wang's accomplices were numerous and spread throughout various key locations. Deng Longguang and Li Hanhun, the commanders of the stationed army divisions, had heard about this for a long time. Recently, Wang's activities became increasingly rampant, colluding with party members in various counties, forming a traitorous group, and providing our military and political information and intelligence data to the ruffians. After Li Hanhun confirmed the facts, he ordered Lin Yan, the regiment commander of the stationed army in Chenghai, to arrest Wang. Wang confessed to colluding with foreign merchants to smuggle goods without denying it. On the 15th, Li had Wang executed by firing squad as a warning to the public. All traitors were terrified, resigned from important positions, and fled. The ruffian organization suffered a fundamental blow.

Guangdong Province Develops Transportation Industry, Construction Department Rushes to Build Major Highways in the Northeast Region, Telecommunications Bureau Unifies Long-Distance Telephone Services in Various Counties 54

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province is urgently developing its transportation industry, and is actively constructing both roads and telecommunications. Currently, the county highways, in addition to the two trunk lines in the eastern region and one trunk line in the southern region, the cross-county roads connecting the various trunk lines have not yet been completed. The first trunk line in the eastern region runs from Guangzhou to Huiyang, and from Huiyang through Huilai and other counties to Shantou; the second trunk line runs from Huizhou, Heyuan, Xingning to Meixian; and the southern trunk line runs from Siyi, through Liangyang, into Gaozhou, and connects to the Qinlian Road. Recently, the Construction Department, in order to improve northeast transportation, decided to build the Wengyuan to Conghua highway and the Conghua to Xinfeng highway in the short term, so that it is possible to reach the North River directly from the eastern region without passing through Guangzhou. The department has sent personnel to survey the routes of the above two roads, and the survey has been completed. As soon as the construction funds are allocated, construction can begin. As for the Shao-Lian Road (i.e., from Shaozhou to Lianxian), which runs from the North River through the Little North River to the Guibian area, it is also planned to be built. After a survey was conducted, the entire line is 340 miles long, and most of the areas along the way are rural, so the construction should not be difficult. However, the estimated construction cost is also more than 900,000 yuan. The Construction Department has already reviewed the budget and drawings, and construction can begin in the short term.

Regarding telecommunications, the Ministry of Communications recently decided to reorganize the plan, and the management of wired and wireless communications has gradually been unified. However, the long-distance telephone services of the various county mayors were originally managed independently, either by the government or by merchants, and the systems were not connected. Although connections between counties have been made over the years, it has not yet become a provincial transportation network. Recently, in order to implement the management of long-distance telephone services throughout the province, the Telecommunications Administration Bureau has sent a commissioner to Shantou to take over the long-distance telephone services operated by merchants in Shantou. In the future, the long-distance telephone services in various counties under the jurisdiction of the Construction Department, such as the Guangzhou-Shantou long-distance telephone line in the eastern region, the Guangzhou-Huiyang line, the Guangzhou-Qingyuan Huaxian line in the central region, and the Guangzhou-Shaozhou line in the northern region, will also be transferred to the management of the Telecommunications Bureau. After the long-distance telephone services throughout the province are unified, it is planned to establish a long-distance telephone central station in Guangzhou and branch stations in various counties. The estimated reorganization cost is 4.5 million yuan. It is said that this telecommunications construction cost has been included in the provincial budget for the 26th year [of the Republic, i.e. 1937]. As for wired communications, efforts are also being stepped up to connect with neighboring provinces, such as the eastern region line connecting with Fujian Province, and the northwest region line connecting with Jiangxi, Hunan, and Guangxi. Recently, the wired telegraph from Guangzhou to Changsha has been reorganized, and telegrams can now be sent directly, which is much more convenient than having to be relayed through other places. (December 21st)

Thorough Investigation of the Chunyi School Disturbance 57

Suzhou Chunyi Middle School was founded by the Lei family, owners of Lei Yunshang Pharmacy, and has been in operation for sixteen years, with over 1,000 students. It is one of the leading private schools in Suzhou. The school principal was Peng Jiazhi, who had served for fifteen years without change. During the summer vacation this year, Gao Runzhong was replaced as principal, so that teachers and staff were greatly mobilized during the autumn semester. Therefore, there was internal strife between the old and the new, and students also had the so-called Peng supporters and Gao supporters, the situation is very complicated. Recently, slogans calling for the expulsion of the principal were found in the school, and disturbances have repeatedly occurred. It is rumored that a part of the students expressed dissatisfaction with the school teacher Zheng Ziyun, and the school's academic director Chen Xulun also resigned. After the Jiangsu Education Department was secretly informed, it sent Zhang Zhukun to Suzhou to investigate. After Zhang arrived in Suzhou, he went to the school to investigate and gave a speech to the students. The truth about the disturbances is already clear, and he returned to the province yesterday to report.

Wuxi: Jindan Case Handed Over to Regional Department 58

The Gan Da Ba Candle Shop outside the North Gate of this county, in the Tan Tou Alley, also sells "Cough Jindan" medicine, which is specially used for treating coughs. It is wholesaled from Yuyao, Zhejiang. Recently, someone suddenly reported to the Administrative Commissioner's Office that the Jindan contains morphine, a poisonous substance. After receiving the report, the Commissioner's Office immediately ordered the Third Public Security Bureau to chemically test the Jindan. It was confirmed to contain poisonous substances. The shop's clerk, Qiu Xirong, was taken to the bureau and presented to the main bureau, which transferred him to the county government for interrogation and detention. Yesterday, the city and county governments jointly sent him to the Second District Security Command for interrogation.

Changshu: Planning to Build a New County Government 59

Civil and criminal litigation cases here are increasing daily, and there is an urgent need to establish a local court. However, there is no suitable location for the Changshu Court, which has caused delays. Now, the Jiangsu High Court has subsidized 35,000 yuan to purchase the current county government building to be used as a court. As for the county government building, it has been decided to rebuild the Shimei Library. The library will be moved to the new park outside the North Gate. This decision has been largely finalized. The court is scheduled to be established on March 1, and all are proceeding with the original plan. As for the library issue, opinions from all sides consider that the new park is too far north, and the location on the mountainside is difficult to manage. The general opinion is that after the merger of the middle school's girls' department, the library should be moved to the Dushutai (Reading Terrace). The location is very suitable, and it also conforms to the historical site of Zhaoming's Dushutai. It is still under discussion.

Zhenjiang: Defining Residential Area for the Poor 60

The Zhenjiang County Government believes that building housing for the poor is urgently needed in modern society. Amidst the current rectification of the city's appearance, there is an even greater need to actively construct it. County Magistrate Zhang is actively working on this issue and has designated locations such as Doutian Temple at the foot of Beigushan Mountain as residential areas. Currently, issues such as fundraising and architectural design are being discussed. As soon as everything is ready, construction can begin.

Nanjing: Salt Industry Raises Funds to Support Suiyuan 61

Since the Suiyuan war broke out, all sectors of Nanjing have risen to provide assistance. "One Day Movement One Dollar" has been strongly promoted, so the remittance of cash and goods to the front lines to provide comfort has been more enthusiastic than in other places. The fundraising for the salt industry is also extremely active. According to the person in charge of the General Salt Association, in addition to the 237 yuan donated by the association and its employees in one day, the Jiuda Salt Company donated 2,000 yuan, the Tongyi Salt Factory donated 600 yuan, the General Manager's Office donated 400 yuan, and the Hankou Salt Industry Association donated 1,000 yuan. The total amount has exceeded 5,000 yuan.

Ningbo: Dahua Steamer Runs Aground on Its Way to Shanghai 62

The Dahua steamer of the Shanghai Baohua Steamer Bureau, which operates between Shanghai and Haimen, left Haimen for Shanghai at around 12:00 PM on the 22nd, carrying 64 passengers and hundreds of pieces of cargo. At 4:00 AM on the 23rd, when the ship was passing the waters of Huangfengzui in Shuangqigang, Liuhong Island, Dinghai, due to thin fog, the visibility was low. The driver, for caution's sake, sailed along Liuhong Island by foot. Unexpectedly, it hit the foot of Huangfeng Mountain, causing one-third of the ship's body to run aground on the foot of the mountain and unable to move. The shipowner hurriedly called for help. At that time, the Nanhai steamer passed by, and hearing the sound, suspected it was a robbery and did not dare to approach immediately, so it anchored and waited. At around 7:00 AM, the tide receded and the sky cleared, revealing the truth. Then it went forward and rescued the Dahua passengers into its own ship. Hong, the Dahua's purser, took the Nanhai to Zhenhai and reported to the Foreign Water Police to send a team to protect it, to prevent pirates from looting. The Dahua steamer could only get out of danger when the tide rose.

Random Jottings of a European Journey 63

— By Our Newspaper's Correspondent in Europe, Lieshan

I. Different Views

It is said that during his time in Germany, Dai Jitao, the President of the Examination Yuan, conducted an on-the-ground investigation of the current situation in Germany, visiting many cities. Once, when traveling to a certain city, the mayor and the local National Socialist Party branch, as usual, hosted a banquet to welcome Mr. Dai as an honored guest. During the banquet, Mr. Dai stood up and gave a speech, half for diplomatic courtesy and half because the achievements of Germany in recent years were indeed worthy of admiration by foreign guests (especially the national defense plan). Therefore, it was naturally unavoidable to say a few words in favor of Germany. Unexpectedly, the next day, the German newspaper recorded the following passage: "(Mr. Dai said) You Germans have given us a model, and we Chinese are very grateful... Our leader Chiang Kai-shek is emulating your leader Hitler..."

I remember a Chinese classmate studying in the Department of Mechanical Engineering, who was usually a good-tempered man, suddenly had a small conflict with a German one day, eventually arguing until they were red in the face. Afterwards, he told the reporter, "Look, isn't this outrageous? Just now that German student actually said to me that what China lacks is a Hitler, saying that our Chiang Kai-shek should learn from their leader Hitler. In fact, our Chiang Kai-shek's talent and ability are many times higher than their Hitler. How many difficult things are there in China? Let Hitler try it. This is simply an insult to us. Our Chiang Kai-shek should learn from their Hitler."

Naturally, different people have different views.

II. Who is China's Greatest Modern Diplomat?

"Weak countries have no diplomacy," but a friend who specializes in international politics used the question "Who is China's greatest modern diplomat?" to make things difficult for me. I said, "Friend, the history of China's modern diplomacy is a history of national disasters. Although we are unwilling to judge heroes by success or failure, but!"

He told me, "If I want to find such a figure in the history of Chinese diplomacy or in the diplomatic world, then my time would be wasted." I said, "He must be outside the history of diplomacy and the diplomatic world," he replied.

In my opinion, there are only two greatest diplomats in modern China. It is hard to say that they are not diplomats, but unfortunately they are both dead: Sun Yat-sen and Hu Hanmin. When Mr. Sun was passing through Japan, the Japanese invited him to give a speech on Pan-Asianism. He did not forget that he was a Chinese. He told the Japanese audience that the premise of Pan-Asianism was whether Japan wanted to Europeanize itself like Europe, or return to Asia and follow China! This has the air of a diplomat. When Mr. Hu was in Moscow, the Communists held a large meeting to welcome him. There was a slogan in the meeting place: "From Sun Yat-senism to Leninism." After Mr. Hu saw it, he immediately said on the spot: "This slogan should be reversed, from Leninism to Sun Yat-senism." Then he explained his views. Talking about Leninism with the Communists in Moscow is a diplomat's courage!

This friend continued, "Diplomats certainly need to have social skills, but people who only have social skills are at most only fit to be embassy staff members."

III. Guo Taiqi's Clever Remark

When the Chinese legation in Britain was promoted to an embassy, the first ambassador, Mr. Guo Taiqi, in accordance with diplomatic practice, had to present his credentials to the King of England. Britain is a country that loves antiques, not only respecting the customs of the days of the old grandmothers, especially the royal etiquette. There is not much difference between the twentieth century and the seventeenth and eighteenth centuries. The young Edward VIII, since childhood, received this kind of family education, and in his dealings with diplomats from other countries, he would not forget the ancestral set of ceremonies. It is said that the King of England also used the old custom at that time, and when presenting the credentials, he said to Mr. Guo: "I have heard that in recent years your country's relations with Japan are not good, and I am worried about it. Our country hopes for world peace, and I hope that your country and Japan can be friendly in the future..." This was reminiscent of the style of a large country's monarch.

This was naturally a difficult problem for Mr. Guo. How to answer? In this solemn situation, how could he discuss the rights and wrongs between China and Japan with the King of England? He only replied coldly, "Fortunately, our China is still large!" Mr. Guo did not laugh when he said this, but Edward VIII, and even the former Foreign Secretary Simon, a most British "cold and colder" figure, finally couldn't help but laugh.

IV. British Home Secretary Simon

The current British Home Secretary Simon is the leader of the right-wing national faction in the Liberal Party. During the Northeast Incident, he was the Foreign Secretary. It is said that he was responsible for the fact that the attitudes of Britain and the United States towards Japan at that time were unable to be consistent. Later, he was transferred to Home Secretary due to the Italian-Ethiopian affair. Home Secretary Simon is a famous British legal expert. Although his political life has been smooth sailing, he does not seem to have become a figure generally loved by the people, especially in the Parliament, where he is often the target of attacks by the opposition. For example, when Prime Minister Baldwin announced the appointment of the Home Secretary in Parliament, a Labor Party member in the House of Commons immediately stood up and questioned the Prime Minister in front of Simon, asking whether the Prime Minister specifically asked him to try his hand at domestic affairs because Simon's handling of foreign affairs had failed!

Home Secretary Simon, although a typical British gentleman, the opposition did not show any concern for this. Therefore, his experience in Parliament was more pitiful than that of other politicians. I remember that in July of this year, when the British House of Commons debated the new law on unemployed workers, Home Secretary Simon also made a speech defending the government. At that time, a Labor Party member suddenly stood up and interrupted his speech, pointing at him and saying, "The Home Secretary is lying." Later, although this member was punished with expulsion, it also aroused the indignation of several Labor Party and Liberal Party members. They loudly told Simon, "We all know that the Home Secretary is a famous liar." Another said, "Everyone knows that you are the most vulgar liar!"

Naturally, this was somewhat of an insult. Even with the political status of the Home Secretary, he could still not resist the opposition, this is the British parliamentary system.

V. Cleverness Overreached

The British are famous for being polite. Chinese people who come to London for the first time will always receive warnings from "old Londoners." The British never like to say bad things about others. Therefore, we Chinese should also return the courtesy and never criticize British things. Remember, even if things are bad, you have to say they are good. For example, on a cloudy day when it is about to rain, you should also say that it is good weather. This is gentlemanly enough!

Once, several Chinese students went to visit a school in a certain British industrial area. Because of the many factories in that area, it has always been known for being unsanitary in Britain, and this school was naturally no exception. When the principal of the school received them, he first apologized to the visitors, saying that the area was very unclean because of the industrial area. The Chinese students at that time did not forget the British gentlemanly courtesy and quickly replied, "Not at all, it is very clean here!" This, in turn, made the principal feel confused. He thought, if the Chinese thought a place like this was very clean, then the daily life of the Chinese people can be imagined!

Not learning to be a gentleman, China ended up suffering instead.

Municipal No. 1 Stadium: Chinese Chess Finals News 74

The first round of the Shanghai Municipal No. 1 Stadium's First Chinese Chess Competition concluded on the 24th. It is also decided that the competition for the top fifteen players (i.e., the first-place winners of each group) will be the Division A final, and the competition for the latter sixteen players will be the Division B final. Both will begin at 7 PM on the afternoon of the 28th of this month. The schedule has been arranged and will be sent out at 5 PM today. All competitors can come to the venue before 5 PM to collect it. It is also reported that each player in both Division A and Division B will have two games each night at 7 PM and 8 PM, so all competitors must attend at 7 PM each night. Furthermore, in this round-robin final, each game will consist of two rounds. Winning one game will earn two points, a draw will earn each player one point, and a loss will earn zero points. The final ranking will be determined by the total number of points, with the highest points ranking first.

Chinese Education Society Resolves to Participate in the World Education Conference 75

(Nanjing, 25th) The Chinese Education Society held a plenary meeting of its directors in Nanjing on the 24th. More than ten people, including Zhang Boling, attended. Chairman Zhang decided on several important cases, the most important of which are as follows: (1) It was decided to solicit educational papers from students of national normal school education departments throughout the country and award prizes. The period for submission of papers is from January 1st to the end of April. (2) The invitation from the National Compilation and Translation Bureau to review and revise educational terms was accepted. The detailed implementation methods will be handled by the Bureau in conjunction with the original Terminology Review Committee of the Society. (3) Preparing to participate in the World Education Conference: A. A letter will be sent to Dr. Monroe again, informing the Society of its readiness to join the World Education Society and requesting a response regarding the amount of membership fees and other information regarding the conference to be held in Tokyo next year. B. A preparatory committee for attending the World Education Conference will be formed. Zhang Boling, Jiang Menglin, Ma Zongrong, and thirteen others were nominated as members. C. Five other groups, including the China Children's Education Society, will be invited to send representatives to participate in the preparation, and a preparatory meeting will be held at the Ministry of Education on January 20th.

Return from Sichuan: Li Denghui Returned to Shanghai Yesterday; Over 200 People Welcomed Him at the Port; Talks About the Amazing Development of Education in Chongqing 79

Dr. Li Denghui, President of Fudan University, left Shanghai on October 17th to visit Sichuan, passing through Nanjing, Wuhan, Chongqing, and Chengdu. He returned to Shanghai yesterday morning at 8 AM aboard the Minsheng Industrial Company's Minquan ship, docking at the Longmao Wharf on Wuma Road. Over two hundred people came to the port to welcome him, including Wu Nanxuan, Vice President of Fudan University, Zhang Yi, Dean of Instruction, Yin Yiwen of the Affiliated Middle School, Zhu Zusun of the Experimental Middle School, Wang Jingzhong, student representative, Wu He from the Fujian Fellow Association in Shanghai, Wu Daocun, representative of the Fudan Alumni Association, military training officers from the university and affiliated middle school, and Li's friends and students. Miss Cheng Huiqing presented flowers, the Boy Scouts stood at attention to show respect, and the school song was sung. Dr. Li gave a brief talk to reporters on the ship, saying that the purpose of his trip to Sichuan was to take a break from the hard work of running the university for many years. He visited Sichuan to visit alumni and investigate the development of education there, so as to learn from it and improve Fudan. The development of education in Chongqing has been rapid in recent years. Although elementary school students there live more than ten miles from school, they also travel back and forth on foot. Their daily life is very simple. The progress in children's education is even better than in Wuhan and other places. As for whether to take the position of legislator, it has not yet been decided. He plans to rest in Shanghai for a few months, and may travel to South China next spring. He is very grateful for the warm welcome from the military and political leaders and alumni in various places during this trip. At noon, Vice President Wu Nanxuan hosted a reception for him at the Laixi Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road to welcome him back. Mr. Zhang Yi will host a reception tonight to welcome him back. The Fudan Alumni Association, faculty, and other groups will also host a reception for Li on another day.

The New Universal Vocational School, New Universal Middle School, New Universal Second Elementary School on Chongqing Road, and New Universal Elementary School on Parker Road in this city celebrated their fourth anniversary yesterday. It is reported that the school will hold an alumni association and sports games at 9 AM today, and a fun fair in the afternoon to entertain guests and student parents, which will be even more grand.

National Beiping Academy of Sciences Geological Research Grant Extended to the End of March Next Year, Letters Sent to Universities for Notification 83

The National Beiping Academy of Sciences recently sent letters to universities in this city, stating that the geological and mineral research grant of the academy has been handled in the past years. Currently, the special grant item is still suspended, and the ordinary grant continues to be handled. Those who submit papers on this topic should submit them to the academy by the end of March of the 26th year of the Republic of China for submission to the review committee for review. Two copies of the rules for the land, geology, and mineral research grant are enclosed. Please check and introduce candidates for papers requesting this grant to submit application forms to the academy in accordance with the format within the deadline for processing.

Scope of the Grant: The scope of the grant is geology, minerals, paleontology, mining, and metallurgy. Types of Grants: Divided into the following two types: (1) Ordinary Grants: College undergraduates in the third or fourth year (or those with equivalent academic qualifications) or college graduates who have preliminary research and achievements in geology, minerals, paleontology, mining, or metallurgy may be given ordinary grants. (2) Special Grants: Those who have special research and important contributions in the above subjects may be given special grants. Distribution of Grants: (1) Ordinary Grants: One-sixth of the total annual grant of 6,000 yuan will be used as ordinary grants, divided into several awards, each ranging from 100 yuan to 500 yuan. (2) Special Grants: Five-sixths of the total grant of 6,000 yuan will be used as special grants, divided into the following two types: Category A: One award of 5,000 yuan; Category B: Divided into awards, each ranging from 2,000 yuan to 3,000 yuan, determined annually by the review committee. If there are no qualified recipients, the award may be suspended, and the grant for that year will be used as a fund, and the method will be determined separately.

Application Procedures: (1) Grant applicants should have research papers for review. If there are inventions or discoveries of physical objects, they should also be reviewed. Research papers should be in Chinese. If the original text of the paper is in a foreign language, a Chinese translation should be attached. (2) Grant applicants may submit applications themselves or be recommended by academic institutions or organizations related to geology and minerals. In either case, two copies of the application form must be filled out in accordance with the prescribed format. The review committee may also award grants if it considers that there are qualified recipients in addition to the above-mentioned self-application or recommendation. Review Procedures: (1) The review committee will meet and resolve the review results of the papers of applicants in the previous year before February 15th each year. The review committee meeting will be convened by the president of the National Beiping Academy of Sciences. (2) The review committee may invite experts outside the committee as temporary consultants. (3) The review results will be decided by a majority vote of all members. (4) The review results will be announced by the National Beiping Academy of Sciences.

Shanghai Celebrates Chiang Kai-shek's Safe Arrival in Luoyang 88

Party and government agencies hire many large cars, setting off firecrackers along the Bund in the Chinese and foreign concessions. The municipal party headquarters announces that the city will fly flags today. The public will hold a general meeting at the municipal chamber of commerce today.

The people of Shanghai were delighted to learn that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, accompanied by Soong Tzu-wen and Madame Chiang Soong Mei-ling, safely arrived in Luoyang by plane at 5:30 p.m. on the 25th, after the Xi'an Incident. Their joy and excitement were indescribable. Newspapers rushed to publish extra editions (this newspaper's extra edition was the first to be published at 6:40 p.m. and distributed along the streets by car). Households, shops, and agencies all set off firecrackers. Dozens of large cars hired by the municipal party headquarters and the municipal government, fully loaded with firecrackers, were set off along the streets in the Chinese and foreign concessions. Radio stations broadcast special programs. Pedestrians on the streets were like weaving fabric, cheering as if crazy. The enthusiasm and joy were unprecedented.

The Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters

learned last night at 6:00 p.m. that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek had indeed safely arrived in Luoyang. It immediately convened a temporary executive committee meeting to discuss celebration methods and resolved: (1) to immediately hire ten cars with large slogans reading "Celebrating Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Safe Arrival in Luoyang" and set off firecrackers to parade throughout the city so that citizens would know that the leader had escaped danger; (2) to notify all agencies, organizations, schools, factories, shops, and residences throughout the city to fly flags today (the 26th) to celebrate; (3) to schedule a celebration meeting; (4) to send a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to celebrate. The following is a record of the announcement of the municipal party headquarters: "For the matter of notification, our party and national leader Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has safely arrived in Luoyang and continues to exercise his powers. Therefore, all citizens of the city are hereby notified to fly the national flag on the 26th of this month (today) to express their celebration. This is a special announcement."

Mayor Wu's Telegram of Condolence

Last night, upon hearing that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek had safely arrived in Luoyang, he sent a telegram of condolence and congratulations, which read: "To Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Luoyang, Your Excellency, your safe escape from danger today is a blessing for the party and the country and a boon to the people. All citizens are celebrating with their hands on their foreheads. I hereby send a telegram to express my respect and inquire about your well-being. Tiedcheng kowtows, with seal."

Heaven blesses the virtuous, which is a great blessing for our country and nation. I have been praying piously day and night, daring not to slacken. Municipal Party Headquarters Convened Yunnan Uprising Commemoration Meeting Yesterday, Chairman Xing Wan Reported the Significance of the Commemoration, City Flew Flags to Commemorate, Chinese Concession on Alert 89

Yesterday (the 25th) was the anniversary of the Yunnan Uprising, the memorial day of overthrowing Hongxian. The authorities of this city specially held a commemoration meeting in the Great Hall of the headquarters at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. Xing Wan was the chairman, Du Mengsen was the recorder, and Zhang Hanyun was the master of ceremonies. The following is a record of the opening meeting:

Venue Arrangement

The venue was set in the auditorium of the Municipal Party Headquarters. The party and national flags and a white cloth banner were hung in front of the gate, with the words "Shanghai All-Circles Representatives Hold Yunnan Uprising 21st Anniversary Commemoration Meeting" written on it. The national flag, party flag, and the portrait of the Prime Minister were hung in the center of the hall. Order slogans were posted on both sides, and slogans were posted all over the four walls. The atmosphere was very solemn.

Representatives Present

Xing Wan of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Jiang Huaisu of the Municipal Defense Committee, Huang Kegui of the Municipal Education Association, Sheng Yizhang of the Foreign Affairs Office, Huang Xianggu of the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession, Zhu Yangwu of the Citizens' Association of the First Special District, Mao Yun of the Citizens' Association of the Second Special District, Bao Huizhong of the Gaochang Temple Citizens' Association, Lin Kecong of the Women's Association, Cai Jinying of the Women's Progressive Association, Zhu Shide of the National Goods Maintenance Association, Hu Shouqi of the South District Citizens' Association, Zhu Yakui of the Lawyers' Association, Yu Yaoqiu of the Baoshan Fellow Villagers Association, Wu Wenbang of the Labor Movement Alumni Association, Chen Duanzhi of New Asia Middle School, Jiang Weixin of East China Girls' High School, and more than 200 representatives from various agencies, organizations, schools, and party headquarters at all levels.

Opening Ceremony

(1) Opening (all stand up); (2) sing the party song; (3) salute the party and national flags and the portrait of the Prime Minister; (4) the chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will; (5) silence; (6) the chairman reports; (7) speech; (8) shout slogans; (9) adjournment.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony, Chairman Xing Wan gave a report, stating: "Yuan Shikai not only destroyed the law and dissolved the Kuomintang, but also dissolved the parliament. After the assassination of Song Jiaoren, the party attempted to overthrow Yuan Shikai, but unfortunately failed. However, this claim was not abandoned and continued to struggle. As a result of the arrangements in various parties, twenty-one years ago today, the Yunnan Uprising was launched to crusade against Yuan Shikai. Yunnan comrades urged Tang Jiyao to denounce, and Cai E and others were appointed to lead troops north. On the 23rd, a telegram was sent to Yuan Shikai to punish the thirteen culprits. Yuan ignored it. Therefore, on the 25th, a declaration was issued to launch an expedition. The provinces responded one after another, which shows that Yuan was not tolerated by the Republic of China. Today's commemoration should recognize the following three points: (1) Revolutionary power is built on the psychology of the masses. If there is a violation, it will fail. For example, Cao Kun's bribery election and the rampant warlords were eventually eliminated. Recently, public opinion has sought domestic unity. If this fact is violated, it will be difficult to survive. The same is true for the Fujian People's Government and the Liangguang issue. Recently, Zhang Xueliang's rebellion in Xi'an detained Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, which violated the national public opinion, not only undermined unity, but also destroyed the outline. At the time of the victorious suppression of bandits in Suiyuan, it was infinitely affected by Zhang Xueliang. If it is not wiped out, it cannot be unified, the outline cannot be rectified, and the nation cannot be revived. (2) The Yunnan Uprising was a great cause of overthrowing the monarchy and rebuilding the Republic of China, and at the same time seeking the implementation of the Three Principles of the People. What our country needs now is a national front. Other doctrines and so-called people's fronts are not in line with national conditions and society. Promoting the people's front, as the name implies, is in opposition to the government and will never succeed. (2) Yuan Shikai's proclaiming himself emperor was Yuan's ambition, but it was also because some comrades in the party could not listen to the commander's instructions, which led to the weakness of the revolutionary forces and the arrogance of the feudal forces. Yuan Shikai took the opportunity to proclaim himself emperor. In order to punish the past and be cautious, we must support the leader and obey the leader. This is a necessary condition at present. This time, the leader suffered in Xi'an, and we used the power of the entire nation to welcome and implement the established national policy."

Flying Flags on Alert

Yesterday was a national memorial day. All agencies, organizations, schools, and various departments in this city, in addition to sending representatives to participate in the commemoration meeting convened by the Party Headquarters and flying flags to commemorate, all remained open as usual and did not take a holiday. The Garrison Command, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the police stations of the two concessions, in view of the current period of martial law, strengthened their defenses and vigilance.

Municipal Public Security Bureau Anti-Drug Propaganda Day 3 91

Since the Municipal Public Security Bureau stepped up and expanded anti-drug propaganda on the 23rd of this month, detailed propaganda has been reported in various newspapers. Yesterday (the 25th) was the third day. The propaganda personnel appointed by the bureau, in addition to setting off to give lectures in accordance with the prescribed areas, also heard that the bureau had investigated and dealt with cases of manufacturing and trafficking of drugs in the North Sichuan Road area of ​​this city. Therefore, it paid special attention to extensively promoting the North Sichuan Road area yesterday, warning the landlords or second landlords there not to provide housing for people who manufacture or traffic drugs, and should pay attention to them at any time and strictly report them. Those who know but do not report, once the bureau catches the case, will detain the drug offenders along with the second landlord and send them to the military law agency for punishment according to law. At the same time, the bureau will step up the investigation and suppression work to ensure that no more drug cases occur in the North Sichuan Road area, in order to achieve the purpose of completely eliminating drugs.

Zou Lu Arrives in Shanghai from Guangdong Yesterday; Zou Discusses the Shaanxi Incident as the Greatest Misfortune for the Nation; Scheduled to Enter Beijing This Morning to Meet with Key Central Figures 92

Central Executive Committee member Zou Lu, returning from his European tour, originally intended to enter Beijing at an early date. However, he remained in Guangdong for medical treatment due to illness. After the Xi'an Incident occurred, Zou was extremely saddened and indignant upon learning of it, so he made a special effort to come north despite his illness to seek a solution. Zou boarded the Changxing Company's Asia Queen liner on the 23rd and arrived in Shanghai at noon yesterday, scheduled to enter Beijing this morning. The details are recorded as follows:

Enthusiastic Welcome

Those who went to the ship to welcome Zou Lu yesterday included Tao Baichuan and Tong Xingbai, representatives from the Central Party Headquarters and the Municipal Party Headquarters; Xu Kan, representative of Vice-President Kong; Li Dachao, representative of Mayor Wu; Wang Zhinan, representative of Yang Hu, Commander of the Songhu Garrison; Central Executive Committee members Hu Wencan and Lu Yougang; Fu Rulin, Chairman of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission; Deng Gang, Director of the Fourth Route Army's Beijing Office; and Xie Zhongfu, Wang Zhisheng, Cao Siwu, Chen Da, and Zou's wife, among others. A banner reading "Welcome Party-State Elder Zou Haibin" was hung on the pier, and the scene was very enthusiastic.

Entering Beijing This Morning

The Asia Queen liner that Zou Lu was on arrived in Shanghai at noon yesterday and docked at the Broadway Road Gonghe Fresh Dock. After briefly socializing with the welcomers on the ship, Zou disembarked and went straight to the Cangzhou Hotel to rest. Zou is scheduled to take an early train to Beijing at 8:00 this morning to join key central figures in discussing how to deal with the Shaanxi Incident. Those who came with Zou Lu yesterday included Central Executive Committee member Luo Yiqun, Wu Zhimei of the Guangdong Provincial Party Committee, Deng Zhiyi, Dean of the Agricultural College of Sun Yat-sen University, and Zou's secretary, Xie Mingzhang, among others.

Zou's Remarks

According to Zou, the Xi'an Incident is the greatest misfortune for the country. The urgent need is to seek a solution to first rescue Chairman Chiang Kai-shek from danger. He had been recuperating in Guangdong due to illness. After hearing of the Xi'an Incident, he immediately made an effort to travel north to work with comrades in the central government to find a response. As for whether he will go to Shaanxi, he has not yet decided. The Third Plenary Session of the Fifth Central Executive Committee will be convened within one or two months. Xiao Focheng is residing in Siam and has not been in contact recently, it is said.

Charitable Organizations' Disaster Relief Association Holds Board Meeting Yesterday; Concrete Plan Passed; Investigating Allocation of 120,000 Yuan 93

The Joint Disaster Relief Association of various charitable organizations in the city held its second standing board meeting at the Renji Hall at 3:00 PM yesterday. Over 30 people attended, including Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Wang Yiting, Xiong Xiling, Du Yuesheng, Qu Wenliu, Pan Gongzhan, Zhang Xiaolin, Cai Jinjun, Li Dachao, Mao Yun, and Zhu Ziqiao. Wang Yiting chaired the meeting, Zhao Cheng recorded the minutes, and the meeting passed fundraising and relief plans. The details are recorded as follows:

Resolutions Passed

(1) The relief group submitted a relief plan (with detailed rules), which was passed item by item. (2) The fundraising group submitted a concrete fundraising plan, which was passed with amendments. (3) The general affairs group submitted a plan for overseas publicity (attached with telegram drafts to major ambassadors and chambers of commerce), which was passed, and efforts to continue appealing and deeply describe the details of the domestic disaster victims were continued. (4) Regarding the case of former relief distribution committee member Yang Zigong, who has gone to Beiping, to immediately distribute relief funds, (5) Regarding the case of the Ministry of Finance allocating 100,000 yuan to the association for disaster relief, and the association should raise some funds to investigate and allocate them together, cases 4 and 5 were discussed and resolved together. The association should first allocate 20,000 yuan, together with the 100,000 yuan from the Ministry of Finance and cold-proof items and medicines, and go to investigate and allocate them immediately. A letter should also be sent to Feng Yangshan to investigate the situation first, so that Qu Wenliu can go to investigate and allocate the funds. (6) Few items have been received by the Zhenpin Office. All Zhenkuan funds should be used to make clothes and quilts in Shanghai, or, after removing the donated Zhenpin items, should be distributed in cash. (Resolution) Except for the donated relief items, everything should be distributed in cash. (7) Should relief vehicles be purchased? (Resolution) The general affairs group and the relief group should consult with the transportation committee to handle this matter. (8) Other temporary motions. (Resolution) Wang Xiaoji, the director of the fundraising group, firmly resigned from his position. Li Dachao was earnestly requested to stay in the position. The association allocated 1,005 yuan to assist the Chinese Buddhist Disaster Relief Group with its start-up expenses. Wang Yiting personally donated 3,000 yuan, and the association donated 2,000 yuan, designated for the Henan region. The meeting adjourned at around 5:00 PM.

Relief Plan

(1) Relief matters will be handled by the Red Cross Society, the Red Swastika Society, the Chinese Buddhist Association, and the disaster area relief team, and concrete measures will be determined. (2) Relief matters will be divided into on-site distribution and en-route relief. The Red Cross Society's relief work should be effectively assisted to promote both sides. (3) Vice-Chairman Qu Wenliu was immediately appointed to personally go to the disaster area to investigate and distribute relief funds, and Yang Zigong and Feng Yangshan and others were sent to investigate and distribute relief funds in advance. (4) The actual situation of relief in various places should be reported to the association by relevant groups or individuals at any time for public announcement.

Fundraising Plan

(1) Fundraising goals: (1) Zhenkuan (relief funds), (2) Zhenpin (relief items). (2) Fundraising methods: (1) Open donation drive with newspaper advertisements, general circulars, and distribution of donation books, (2) Charitable organizations pledging donation amounts (regardless of Zhenkuan or Zhenpin), (3) The association's founders, chairmen, vice-chairmen, standing committee members, and committee members will be responsible for soliciting a certain amount of Zhenkuan and Zhenpin, (4) Soliciting donations from wealthy individuals and households, which requires convening meetings for discussion, (5) Requesting the government to allocate a large sum of money to be distributed in the disaster area (reserved), (6) Fundraising extensively from overseas Chinese around the world.

Design Plan

(1) The proposal will be passed and submitted to the general assembly for discussion and implementation. (2) Regarding the rice, wheat, clothing, medicines, and other items donated and purchased, a joint request will be made to the government with other disaster relief groups for free transportation to the war zone. (3) District fundraising methods: (A) Refer to the previous methods of universal fundraising for flood relief by the city's Boy Scouts, (B) Contact various girls' schools to jointly launch fundraising efforts, (C) Publicly recommend Chen Tiesheng and Wang Zhenchang to formulate a detailed organizational plan for district fundraising. (4) Temporarily use the Shanghai Children's Welfare Association as the office address for the design special committee, and the YWCA as the meeting location. (5) Publicly recommend Mrs. Niu Huisheng to convene a plenary meeting on a regular basis for active implementation.

Research on Income Tax on Deposit Interest; Banking Industry Prepares Report; Will Submit for Approval at Joint Meeting; Money Industry to Adopt New Accounting System Starting Next Year 96

Regarding the income tax on deposit interest, research committees from both the banking and money industries have conducted separate research and exchanged views with members of both associations. Now, after referring to the opinions of various banking and money industry associations and member banks and shops, a report has been drafted. It has been decided to hold another joint meeting of the two associations before the end of the month to submit it for approval and then submit it to the Ministry of Finance for contribution. However, regarding the income tax on deposits in foreign banks in China, it is hoped that it will be levied at the same time as Chinese banks and money shops. As for various money shops, except for Fuyuan and others, they all use the old-style accounting system. It has now been decided to uniformly switch to the new-style accounting system starting next year to facilitate calculation.

He'an and Lixin Liners Sailing from Lake to Shanghai Are Robbed; Captains of Both Liners Arrive in Shanghai to Report; Industry Association Cables for Strict Apprehension of Robbers 99

The He'an liner of the China Merchants Inland River Shipping Bureau and the Lixin liner of the Lixin Shipping Bureau, which specialize in sailing small inland river liners from Shanghai to Huzhou and Qian, were robbed on the morning of the 23rd while sailing from Lake to Shanghai when they reached Zhujia浜, 15 miles away from Yuhui. The total loss was approximately 500 yuan. The industry association has cabled for strict apprehension. The details are as follows:

He'an Encounter The He'an liner of the China Merchants Inland River Shipping Bureau sailed from Huzhou with cargo and passengers at 10:00 AM on the 23rd. At 10:30 PM, it reached Zhujia浜, 15 miles away from Yuhui, when 16 robbers speaking Jiangbei and Shanghai accents, traveling on boats, fired shots to force it to stop. The captain was forced to stop the liner under duress. The robbers, armed with rifles and pistols, rushed onto the liner and robbed the 50-plus passengers, resulting in a total loss of over 300 yuan.

Lixin Affected The Lixin liner of the Lixin Shipping Bureau sailed from Huzhou with cargo and passengers at noon on the 23rd, towing a pleasure boat. At 12:00 AM, it reached Zhujia浜, where the captain saw the He'an liner docked. Initially, he thought it was due to mechanical failure, so he continued to move forward as usual, resulting in being robbed as well. The passengers lost approximately 150 yuan. As for the three Westerners in the pleasure boat, the four shotguns they were carrying were also robbed.

Report to Water Police At 1:00 AM on the 24th, the robbers, having looted to their satisfaction, left in their original boats. Afterwards, the captains of the He'an and Lixin liners jointly reported to the Yuhui Water Police Team, requesting them to quickly send police to pursue and apprehend the robbers. When the police arrived, the robbers had already fled far away without a trace. Thereupon, the He'an and Lixin liners continued to sail to Shanghai as usual. The He'an arrived in Shanghai at 11:00 AM, and the Lixin arrived at 4:00 PM. The captains of both liners immediately reported the robbery to the Shanghai Bureau. On the afternoon of the 25th, they sailed to Lake as usual according to schedule.

Cables for Strict Apprehension Furthermore, the Hengji liner of the China Merchants Inland River Bureau and the Licheng liner of the Lixin Shipping Bureau sailed from Shanghai to Lake on the same day. Fortunately, they were not robbed when passing through Zhujia浜 and arrived safely in Huzhou. As for the Inland River Liner Industry Association, after receiving reports from members of the Li and Ju Bureaus, it has cabled the water police of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, urging them to quickly take measures for strict apprehension and send police to protect the shipping, so as to maintain transport and ensure the safety of passengers.
