Shanghai's First Warehouse Opens Today; Tea and Refreshments Served for Visitors; Interior Facilities Well-Equipped 101

The South Shanghai City Warehouse, built by the Shanghai Public Works Bureau, has been completed. The opening ceremony will be held at 2:00 PM on the 26th, with invitations for visitors from all sectors. The details are recorded as follows:

First Warehouse

The Shanghai Municipal Government, considering that the South Shanghai area lacked a scientific warehouse, which caused inconvenience for stacking goods, began designing and building the city's first warehouse in the first half of last year. After selecting the location at the intersection of Xinmatou Street, outside the 16th Pier in South Shanghai, construction began in June of this year. After several months of continuous progress, the project has recently been completed.

Interior Facilities

As for the warehouse, being Shanghai's first warehouse, it is divided into five floors, built with steel and reinforced concrete. Each floor has an area of 11,600 square feet, with a total capacity of 5,000 tons. The total construction cost is 210,000 yuan in national currency. The interior facilities include an elevator that can carry a load of two tons, automatic fire extinguishers, automatic fire doors, unloading machines, etc., which are quite well-equipped. A ten-year contract has been signed with Minsheng Industrial Company for its use.

Invitation Today

The warehouse project was contracted by Dong Ruihe Construction Company. After starting construction in June of this year, it has now been completed. The Municipal Public Works Bureau has specifically invited visitors from all sectors for today (the 26th), sending out invitation cards that read: "The South Shanghai City Warehouse has now been completed. We invite visitors from all sectors to visit at 2:00 PM on Saturday, December 26th. We will prepare tea and refreshments and await your presence. Xu Peixiang. The location is No. 53, Matou Road, South of Maojia Alley, South Shanghai. Admission by invitation."

On the Shanghai-Hankou Section of the Yangtze River, Water Levels Rise Again; A Shoal is Discovered at Madang; All River Steamers Must Detour; Yesterday's Draft Limit: Seventeen Feet 102

The Datong News Agency reports that the water volume in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River is gradually rising again, and Shanghai-Hankou river steamers can navigate without obstruction. However, in the upper reaches of Chongqing and the middle reaches of Yichang, water levels are still falling, indicating shallowness and drought. A Datong News Agency reporter inquired with the Customs Maritime Department yesterday to learn about the situation, which is recorded below:

River Water Rises Again

According to a report from the Datong News Agency, which inquired yesterday with the Jianghai Customs Maritime Department, the water level along the Shanghai-Hankou section of the lower reaches of the Yangtze River has gradually risen again. The water level in Hankou yesterday was already seven feet (the lowest level a few days ago was just over three feet); the water level in Jiujiang was measured at nine feet nine inches; the water level in Anqing was measured at eight feet three inches; and the water level in Wuhu was measured at five feet three inches (the lowest level a few days ago was just over two feet).

Navigation is Unobstructed

Regarding the draft limit for the Shanghai-Hankou section, the Maritime Department announced yesterday that it is seventeen feet three inches for the Wuhu to Jiujiang section, and fifteen feet nine inches for the Jiujiang to Hankou section. Therefore, river steamers traveling to and from Wusong to Hankou can now navigate without obstruction, to the delight of shipping merchants. However, the Customs received a report yesterday on the water level in Yichang in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River, which has receded to only inches. The water level in Chongqing in the upper reaches is also becoming shallower day by day, so navigation in the middle and upper reaches is on the verge of being suspended.

Shoal Discovered

The Maritime Department has discovered a shoal in the Madang Channel, and navigation must detour around it. A notice was issued yesterday afternoon stating: "A shoal has been discovered at the lower end of the Mafu Channel in the Jiujiang section. Its position is one and a half nautical miles above the Quan Yuzhou lighthouse and one chain away from the right bank. The depth of the water above the shoal is 8.5 feet higher than the Jiujiang water level." Navigation guidance: Maintain a distance of one chain from the bank, pass through the Quanxingzhou lighthouse, and then gradually turn the helm outwards, maintaining a distance of one and a half chains from the right bank.

Defense Corps Platoon Leader Captures a Ferocious Bandit with His Bare Hands 103

The Defeng Chicken and Duck Company at the Dada Wharf in Nanshi was robbed by four bandits on the morning of the day before yesterday, suffering significant losses. Police and bandits exchanged gunfire on the scene, and three bandits were captured. One bandit, named Zhang Arong, was shot in the right leg. Later, he pried open the wooden fence at the location and fled towards Dada Lane. Coincidentally, Tang Fusheng, a platoon leader of the South District Defense Corps headquarters, passed by and saw this, so he bravely stepped forward and captured him with his bare hands, seizing a pistol with serial number 5748. He handed him over to the police for interrogation. Yesterday, four male and female bandits were apprehended. The pursuit and investigation of accomplices is currently underway.

The Yin Bengen Assassination Case Still Unable to Open Debate; Because the Case is Exceptionally Complex; Witnesses Must Be Summoned for Further Interrogation 104

Yin Bengen, a native of Anhui who formerly served as a detective in the French Concession police, was assassinated on the night of October 1st this year in front of the home of Shao Wang at No. 168 Wujia Lane, Jiatang, on the border of the French Concession. The French Concession police have now arrested the suspects, Wang Dianhua (also known as Wang Laowu), Wu Weicai, the woman Sun Ergu, and eleven other suspects. After being transferred to the Special Second Court for investigation, eight people who were found to be unrelated were requested to be released. Wang, Wu, and Sun Ergu were requested to be indicted after an extended period of investigation. Subsequently, it was clarified that Sun Ergu was not involved, and she was released without indictment. Wang Dianhua and Wu Weicai were indicted for aiding and abetting murder under Article 271 of the Criminal Code. Wang also confessed that he went with Wang Fufu and Ma Changfu, who are currently at large, to kill Yin. The court ordered a postponement to appoint lawyers for debate and further review. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Wang Gangxu and Prosecutor Wang Ren came to the Second Criminal Court to continue interrogating the two defendants, Wang and Wu. After being indicted, they were transferred to the detention center. Therefore, during this interrogation, both Wang and Wu reversed their testimonies and denied everything, repeatedly claiming innocence and stating that their previous confessions were due to unbearable torture by the police, and they had no choice but to confess, requesting a detailed investigation. Wang also claimed that he was a close friend of the deceased, who ate and slept at his home. If he wanted to kill him, everyone in his family could have done it; why would he have to harm him at Qianjiatang? On the night of the incident, he went with Yin to the home of Shao Wang at Yinjia Tang. Yin played mahjong, and he watched for about an hour. Because his wife was sick, he went home. If he had murdered Yin, wouldn't he have moved and fled? How could he still live in the same place? Wu also denied plotting to kill Yin. Sun Ergu confessed that she had had an affair with Yin Bengen and did not know Wang Laowu. Furthermore, Wu Liaoxiang, a native of Anhui who was Sun Ergu's former lover and is currently serving a four-year and two-month sentence for theft, testified that he did not know Yin Bengen or Wang Laowu. He stated that he did not know if Yin had informed on him, leading to his case. Shao Wang testified that the mahjong game at her house had already ended that night. The deceased fled to her house, and a short person chased in, dragged the deceased out to the door, and then the defendant Wang Diansan opened fire. She said that Wang was wearing a long black gown and a hat resembling a copper basin. She saw his face clearly, but she did not see the short person's face clearly. The court reviewed the testimonies and determined that the case was complex and could not open for debate. The court ordered a postponement to 2:00 PM on the 31st for further interrogation, and also instructed the police to find Shao Wang and the other mahjong players who were there that night to testify.

News from the Courts: Shi Liang is Still in Shanghai; Lawyers Tang and Zhang Cannot Find Her; Requesting the Court's Guidance 105

Shi Liang, a female lawyer who was arrested at the same time as Shen Junru, Wang Zao Shi, Sha Qianli, Li Gongpu, Zhang Naiqi, Zou Tao fen, and six others, left Shanghai and went into hiding after being released on bail from the Third Branch of the High Court and has not yet returned. The Procuratorate of the Special Second Court has repeatedly summoned lawyers Tang Hao and Zhang Zhirang, who were responsible for guaranteeing her release, to court for questioning, and ordered them to pay a cash guarantee of 500 yuan each, with a deadline to find Shi and bring her to court. Lawyers Tang and Zhang have placed advertisements in the newspapers three times, urging Shi to surrender as soon as possible. Lawyer Tang Hao also went to Suzhou to search for her, but without any news. Details have been recorded in this newspaper. At 1:00 PM yesterday, the Chief Prosecutor of the Special Third Court opened a hearing to summon lawyers Tang and Zhang, who appeared on time. The official asked, "Is Shi Liang in court today?" Tang Hao replied, "After the last adjournment, because Lawyer Zhang had matters in Shanghai, I went to Suzhou on Monday. I first inquired at the High Court, but there was no trace of Shi. Then I went to the Hengjie Detention Center in Wuxian County, which is where Shen Junru and the six others are currently detained. There is no women's detention center there, so I went to the High Court Detention Center on Siqian Street to inquire, but Shi Liang was not there either. I then went to find No. 80 Guanqian Street, which turned out to be the Zhongnan Bank, not a shop or residence. There was nothing to be found. I returned to Shanghai and discussed it with Lawyer Zhang, and we placed another advertisement in the newspaper, urging Shi to surrender. So far, there is still no news. We also very much hope that Shi will return to court as soon as possible to fulfill our responsibility." He presented a copy of the newspaper as evidence. Lawyer Zhang Zhirang stated, "We received a letter last time saying that she could come to court in a week, but she has not yet surrendered. We have tried our best to find her, but it is difficult to meet with her." The official said, "According to the court's investigation, Shi Liang is in Shanghai and has not left. Do you have any way to urge Shi to come to court? Otherwise, this court will also find it difficult to see you." Lawyers Tang and Zhang replied, "We have used all possible methods. If the court has any method, please guide us so that we can proceed accordingly." As a result, the court ordered Tang and Zhang to remain under the original guarantee, pending further review.

Female Teacher at Jinan University Attempts Suicide Due to Emotional Distress; Life is in Grave Danger 106

Ms. Zhang Zhenhe, a female teacher at the Affiliated Middle School of National Jinan University in Zhenru, is from Hefei, Anhui. Recently, due to setbacks in her love life, she lost all hope. Around noon yesterday, she secretly swallowed sleeping pills in her dormitory, intending to commit suicide. She immediately lay down on her bed and did not get up. Towards dusk, moaning sounds were heard coming from her room. Several female students entered the room and, seeing the situation, were greatly alarmed. They urgently hired a car to take her to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road for treatment. It is reported that she had taken too many drugs and her life is in extremely critical condition. As for the truth of her emotional distress, those who accompanied her are keeping it secret, so it is impossible to find out.

Cook Dies of Coal Gas Poisoning at Female Doctor's Home 107

Dong Bingrong, a 46-year-old native of Zhenjiang, was employed as a cook at the home of Ms. Lin Huizhen, a gynecologist from Fujian, at No. 1412, Lane 2, Xiafei Road. At 7:20 PM the day before yesterday, while cooking in the kitchen, Dong became poisoned by the coal stove due to the strong heat, and he felt a headache, fainted, and fell to the ground. The owner immediately reported to the police and summoned an ambulance to send him to Guangci Hospital, but he died before treatment could be administered. The body was transferred to the coroner's office. The next day, the Special Second Court was notified, and Prosecutor Wang Ren came to the office to examine the body, confirming that he had died from coal gas poisoning. The body was handed over to the Tongren Fuyuantang to be returned to the family for funeral arrangements.

Silver Flowers and Fiery Trees: Westerners in Shanghai Celebrate Christmas Merrily; Christmas Scenes and Carols Fill the Streets All Night; Church Bells Ring in Unison as Crowds Flock to Worship 108

Yesterday (the 25th) was Christmas, the Western holiday celebrating the birth of Jesus. Foreign nationals and Chinese and foreign Christians in the city celebrated enthusiastically as usual. Consulates, foreign banks, schools, and companies were closed for one or two days. Churches throughout the city began ringing their bells and holding holy masses from the night before (Christmas Eve). Yesterday morning, Christians gathered to hold Christmas services and worship, and the joyous atmosphere was no less than in previous years. The details are as follows:

Fiery Trees and Silver Flowers, Bells Ringing for Holy Mass

Western-owned shops and Chinese and foreign churches in the city began decorating several days before Christmas. Scenes were set up everywhere with holly and electric lights. The shop windows of foreign shops and Chinese businesses, such as Sincere, Wing On, Sun Sun, Dah Sun, and Lihua, on Xiafei Road, Jing'an Temple Road, Nanjing Road, Szechuan Road, Yuyuan Road, and North Szechuan Road in the concession areas, displayed Santa Claus figures and holly snow scenes. At night, the fiery trees and silver flowers were dazzling and beautifully decorated. Each church held a pre-Christmas Eve holy mass at midnight yesterday morning (i.e., midnight), and the bells rang in unison, with hymns being sung, which was quite pleasant.

Westerners Take Holidays, Christmas Worship

On the Western side, consulates, organizations, schools, banks, and shops of various countries in Shanghai were closed yesterday and the day before. Chinese and foreign Christians gathered in churches everywhere yesterday morning to hold solemn Christmas worship services. Christmas worship is one of the four major worship services of the Catholic Church. At the Jiangxi Road Catholic Church, the Mulhall Church on Sanma Road, the Baptist Church on Minguo Road, the Catholic Church on Xiafei Road, and St. Peter's Church on Avenue Haig, the bishops and pastors gave sermons during the worship service. Believers from all over came to listen. The bells rang loudly, and hymns were sung in accompaniment. The solemn and enthusiastic scene was no less than in previous years.

Singing and Dancing All Night, Revelry Until Dawn

All entertainment venues in the city, such as cinemas, dance halls, and bars, were packed on this once-a-year Christmas holiday, and business was booming. All large and small dance halls were specially permitted by the concession authorities to remain open all night on the previous two days. In order to attract business, they also prepared free gifts such as toy paper hats. As a result, Christmas gifts and various toys in companies and shops were twice as profitable. Major hotels such as the Cathay, International, Lido, Grand Cathay, Paramount, and Racecourse Hotel had special musical programs to entertain guests. Amidst the melodious music, the scent of perfume and the gleam of hairpins, the shadows of dancers swayed. The light of jewelry and dresses intertwined. People enjoyed themselves all day long and reveled until dawn, forgetting the urgency of the world's situation, as if they were in a prosperous age. Looking back on the past, I am deeply moved.

Two Railway Lines Suspend Sunday Special Trains Starting January 1, 1937 109

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration previously added special express passenger trains between Shanghai and Wuxi on Sundays, starting from October 25th of this year, in order to facilitate tourists visiting the Suzhou and Wuxi areas. According to the new timetable, there will be a Capital Express train at 8:00 AM and a Shanghai-Nanjing Express train at 8:35 AM departing from the North Station, and a Nanjing-Shanghai Express train at 7:10 PM and a Capital Express train at 8:31 PM departing from Wuxi Station. This is already very convenient for tourists visiting Suzhou and Wuxi, so the Sunday special passenger trains will be suspended starting January 1, 1937.

Counties Intensify Winter Defense 116

The Shanghai County Government, considering that the weather is currently very cold and it is the peak period for intensifying winter defense, and fearing that petty thieves may take the opportunity to commit crimes, has ordered the winter defense offices in each district to strictly prevent crimes in order to maintain public order. Accordingly, the police have been dispatched to routinely inspect inns, teahouses, and taverns within their respective jurisdictions. Travelers with suspicious appearances are subject to thorough questioning at train and ship stations. Police officers in various townships patrol day and night, and security teams are stationed in key areas along the coast.

Chinese and Western detectives of the General Patrol Room previously learned that there was a large gang of Russian thieves who had committed numerous crimes in Tianjin and fled to Shanghai, where they continued their activities, plotting wrongdoing. Starting Next Year, Coal and Stone Lighterage Fees Will Increase; Notice Has Been Sent to the Coal Industry Association for Review 119

The coal and stone lighterage industry in Shanghai has decided to increase the lighterage fees for short-distance transportation starting next year. The industry association has issued a notice stating: "The various shipping companies have reported that in recent years, prices of all goods have been rising, resulting in supply not meeting demand. The various expenses of our shipping industry have also continued to increase, making it difficult to maintain operations. Not only is our shipping industry like this, but other industries are also increasing prices one after another to compensate. Therefore, our shipping industry has no choice but to increase the lighterage fees for short-distance transportation in this port by a certain amount in order to maintain our capital." The notice was submitted to the temporary executive committee meeting on December 6, which resolved that the reports of the shipping companies were indeed factual and that the lighterage fees for short-distance transportation in this port should be increased by five cents per ton from the original price, effective from January 1, 1937. The association has already asked the Shanghai Coal Industry Association to forward the notice to all coal merchants for review.

Shen Laisheng Sues for Encroachment After Brother's Widow Remarries 120

Shen Laisheng, a resident of Yinhang Township in the city center, whose family was originally quite wealthy, suffered during the January 28th Incident when the area was in the war zone. His houses were destroyed in the bombing, and his parents were killed. Only Shen Laisheng and his younger brother Rong Sheng escaped with great difficulty. According to Shen Laisheng, his younger brother only managed to take out four pieces of paper with the title deed to over ten mu of ancestral farmland, along with the grain strings, and sent them to the home of his younger brother's uncle-in-law, Xu Mao Mao. However, his younger brother died soon after, and his brother's widow, Shen Xu, remarried Yu Xiaojiu and openly took her daughter, Tao Mei, as a drag-along child. She also took all the land deeds and conspired with the local security guard, Zhou Jutang, to sell or pawn them all. Based on this, he filed a complaint with the local court against Zhou Jutang and Shen Xu and others for encroachment and sale. The complaint also stated that his younger brother had passed away and had no heirs, so his son inherited the property. At that time, due to the destruction of the home in the war, no division of property was made. Later, his brother's widow said that she was a young widow and should have a means of livelihood, so she asked for a division of property before remarrying. Now that she has broken her promise and committed adultery with someone and remarried, it constitutes encroachment and should be dealt with according to the law. The case was heard yesterday by Judge Wu. The defendant's lawyer Yan Song argued that all the property had already been divided with the help of the aunt, Lu Mao Mao, in July last year, and the title deeds were each held, and the dispute had been resolved. It was clearly a malicious accusation. The official considered the contents to be complex and postponed the hearing to summon witnesses for further interrogation.

Hsiao Ming Girls' Middle School Thrift for Suiyuan Relief 122

Since hearing the good news last month that the National Army was fighting bandits and puppets in Suiyuan, all teachers and students of Hsiao Ming Girls' Middle School of the Catholic Church in this city have been greatly encouraged and immediately launched a thrifty movement to aid Suiyuan, saving money on snacks, cosmetics, pocket money, and transportation expenses to help the soldiers on the front line. Later, it was learned that the Guisui Public Hospital, run by the Catholic Church in the front, had taken in many wounded soldiers and was in urgent need of funds. The first phase of the thrift expenses was settled, totaling $115.10, which was entrusted to Father Cao Aitang Lei to be directly remitted to Guisui. Now, a letter of thanks has been received from Father Fei Huaiyong, the president of the Public Hospital, informing that there are still more than 60 seriously wounded people in the hospital waiting for treatment, including warriors wounded in the battles of Zugertu and Bailingmiao, many of whom have broken legs and arms. Some have their dental arches dislodged, becoming disabled, which is unbearable to witness. The donations received will be completely distributed to the wounded soldiers for treatment and comfort. Soldiers bravely defend the territory, and once they are injured and disabled, they are ignored, which is inhumane. Donating money to help wounded soldiers is not only a good deed but also a patriotic expression. After receiving the letter, all teachers and students of the school were deeply moved and transferred the money for Christmas and New Year's greeting cards and candies, totaling $119.71, directly to Guisui Public Hospital to provide relief to disabled veterans.

Lu Lihua's Report on Investigating National Products: Local Movements are Developing Rapidly, Contributing Opinions in Four Steps 124

Ms. Lu Lihua was commissioned by the National Products Joint Association to investigate the status of the National Products Movement in Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei provinces. She has now completed the task and returned to Shanghai. She specially reported the investigation process to the association. The following is an excerpt from Ms. Lu's report: Lihua departed from Shanghai on the 15th of last month to inspect Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan provinces, investigating the status of the National Products Movement in various places and promoting the National Products Movement. First, she passed through Wuhu, which is the commercial center of Anhui Province. They strongly promote the National Products Movement. There is a National Products Ten-Day Newspaper, a National Products Road, and a small-scale National Products Company to sell domestic products. However, the National Products Movement Association is still lacking. After arriving in the port, I discussed with Administrative Commissioner Gao Wenbo, and the Commissioner's Office hosted a meeting of representatives from all walks of life to prepare for the organization. Fifteen groups attended, and I contributed my humble opinions on the spot, which were deeply appreciated. As a result, it was decided to publicly recommend nine preparatory committee members to form a preparatory committee first, and then establish the National Products Movement Promotion Association. Anqing is the capital of Anhui Province, and its commerce is inferior to Wuhu. Although there is no organization of the National Products Association in the area, they also pay close attention to the National Products Movement. After my arrival, I consulted with the authorities, and the Provincial Party Headquarters hosted a meeting of various institutions, groups, schools, etc., to organize the Anhui Provincial National Products Promotion Preparatory Committee. Jiujiang is an important commercial port in Jiangxi, and a National Products Movement Promotion Association has been established, which was organized by Lin Bingzhou, the brigade commander of the First Independent Brigade of the Navy Marine Corps stationed there, in conjunction with all sectors of society. Military-civilian cooperation is commendable. Wuhan is an important town in Central China, and its commerce has always been developed. The Hankou National Products Movement is led by Mayor Wu Guozhen. There is now a National Products Company and a National Products Movement Committee, which is organized by 15 institutions and groups, including the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Pacification Commissioner's Office, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. The chairman is Yi Baoxun. There is no National Products Movement organization in the Wuchang area. This decision was made by Cheng Jubao of the Department of Education after the inspection, and gathered various institutions and groups to prepare for the organization, and agreed to contact the Hankou National Products Movement Committee to organize the "Hubei Provincial National Products Movement Joint Association" for preparation. The venue is temporarily set up in the Provincial Science Experiment Museum, and it should be established soon. The Hunan People's Patriotic National Products Promotion Association in Changsha is organized by various departments, groups, and organizations of the Hunan Provincial Party, Government, Military, and Police. There is also a large-scale exhibition hall that also sells domestic products. The construction cost is more than 700,000 yuan, and the collection of domestic products is very good. The business is also very developed, and it can be called a force in the Hunan National Products Circle. At the same time, the Shanghai China National Products Company has already set up a branch in the area, and the scale is fairly complete. Looking at the National Products Movement in various places, it can be said that it is quite developed, and the organizers are also working hard. However, what is regrettable is that (1) the authorities have not been able to provide full support, (2) there is a lack of funds, and the established plans are not easy to implement, (3) some of the work is not practical, and (4) the National Products organizations in various places are different, the names are confused, and they cannot be linked consistently to carry out large-scale movement work. Lihua's perception is that there should be four steps to promote national products: (1) Investigate the local production and consumption of national products, (2) Promote the improvement of national products, (3) Enable people to develop the ability to identify national products and non-national products, (4) Universally practice national products. At the same time, the name and organization should be unified, and the highest organ should be set up nationwide to oversee its completion. Provincial, municipal, county, and township areas should set up branch associations. This system is clear, the organization is unified, and the power is consistent, which can achieve the effect of fingers and arms. Annual activity plans should be formulated and implemented step by step, from the center to the township area, nationwide unity, and work results will be even more impressive.

Central Commendation for Xue Hongchang's Generous Support for Suiyuan Cotton Clothes 125

Comrade Xue Hongchang, a member of the 35th Branch of the Second District of this city, paid for the production of 1,000 silk cotton vests and raised 2,000 more from relatives and friends, which were sent to the Municipal Party Headquarters to be forwarded to the Central Government. China Foreign Famine Relief General Association Organizes and Manages the Minsheng Canal Project to Completion, Both Projects Have Been Announced Separately 126

The Suisui Minsheng Canal is one of the achievements of the work-for-relief project of the China Foreign Famine Relief General Association at 505 Henan Road in this port. It was excavated in the autumn of 1928 and lasted four years, with a total construction cost of 750,000 yuan, before it was handed over to the Suiyuan Provincial Water Conservancy Association for management to complete the western project. Later, due to financial constraints, it was virtually suspended, resulting in silting over time, making irrigation difficult. In September of this year, the Famine Relief Association re-discussed dredging and ordered engineer Zhang Jichun to take 15,000 yuan to Tuheqi, Sarachi County, to set up an office, and together with the local authorities, recruited for the reorganization. Since the start of construction, the project has progressed very smoothly. Within a month, most of it was completed. On October 19, water was introduced into the canal, with an average depth of six feet, and the flow was very smooth. From then on, nearby fields can be irrigated, and farmers are all happy.

After the Dahua Ship Ran Aground, the Goods Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday by the Taizhou Ship, the Company Will Send the New Baohua Tomorrow to Tow and Salvage 127

After the Shanghai-Taiwan Qian Dahua ship of the Ping An Shipping Company ran aground at Liuzhushan Mouth, Shuangqikou, Dinghai, the passengers were completely rescued by the Nanhai ship of the Ningbo Nanhai Shipping Company and safely arrived in Dinghai Ningbo. As for the cargo of oranges and the like, a total of 2,000 pieces, it has been unloaded and transported to Dinghai. It was transferred to the Shanghai-Taiwan Qian Taizhou ship of the Taizhou Shipping Company and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. Manager Li Yaoting of the company reported to Shanghai by telegram yesterday morning that although Dahua had run aground, it is expected to be out of danger when the tide rises, and it was decided to send the company's Ningbo Wenzhou Qian New Baohua ship to sail from Yong to the accident site tomorrow for towing and salvage.

Baoshan Seawall Now Under Construction, Provincial Government Allocates 90,000 Yuan, Establishes Engineering Office 128

The Songkou Baoshan seawall is a water conservancy barrier for several counties, including Songhu Jiatai, and is of great importance to farmland irrigation. Therefore, the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Engineering Office, in view of the need to strengthen the seawall and avoid water disasters, after dispatching personnel for inspection, drafted an implementation project plan for the construction of the seawall, which has been approved by the province and allocated a total project cost of 90,000 yuan, including Songtai sections, and established an engineering office in Baoshan, appointing Liu Yeqiu as director. The project started construction the day before yesterday to repair the dangerous sections of Shidong Chucheng Jing, etc.

Post Office Uses Telephone Notification, Methods for Collecting Parcels 130

The Shanghai Postal Administration announced: "In order to expedite parcel delivery, this Bureau has formulated methods for notifying recipients by telephone to come to the Bureau to collect parcels. The provisional regulations formulated are listed below for general knowledge. This announcement is for (1) This method is limited to domestic bulk parcels. (2) Business firms that often receive large numbers of parcels and wish to enjoy this right may apply to this Bureau for registration. The registration fee is one yuan in national currency per firm, and postage stamps should be affixed and canceled on the application form. (3) Once a business firm is registered, it should designate one or more persons to be responsible for collecting parcels, obtain three 4-inch photos of the parcel collector, and obtain one or more postal identity cards from this Bureau for authentication when collecting parcels. (4) The price of each postal identity card is 50 cents. The name and seal of the recipient must be affixed to the card, and the seal must be affixed to the parcel receipt as proof that the recipient has properly received the parcel. (5) If the person dispatched by the recipient to collect parcels needs to be changed frequently, the newly dispatched person must hold another identity card. (6) Business firms enjoying this right should write the registration number in clear font on the parcel skin and the related tax return form, in addition to the required address. (7) If the parcel is not collected within two days after being notified by telephone for collection one or more times, the collection notice will be issued as usual. Director Zha Peilin, December 25, 1936."

National Products Movement Joint Association Continues Visitation Work 131

The household visitation work organized by the National Products Movement Joint Association of this city has been carried out since Xu Chengqing, Xu Songzi, Chen Yingfen, Lin Wen, and Shen Wenxian were selected as visitors to talk to families and persuade them to use national products. They all praised the products of various factories that were brought along. If there were any dissatisfaction, they also criticized frankly. The association has compiled the comments into statistics and published them as follows: praised 852 families, very good 98 families, progress 22 families, poor color 11 families, poor style 20 families, poor pattern 9 families, not strong 109 families, easy to stretch 56 families, poor quality 70 families, other dissatisfaction 53 families, regression 10 families, inferior to foreign goods 19 families, price too expensive 238 families, suspected of not being national products 30 families, lack of politeness 18 families, do not imitate Europe and the United States 6 families, poor fragrance 8 families, need to be improved 14 families, can replace foreign goods 17 families, not bad 13 families. In addition, the household visitation work of the association was originally scheduled to end on January 15, 1937. Now, because the visitation area is not yet universal, it has been submitted to the fourth executive committee meeting for discussion, and it has been decided to include it in the work outline for the next year and continue to carry it out.

Blacksmithing and Straw Bag Prices Increase 132

Recently, various prices in this port have increased, and the cost of living index has risen sharply. Yesterday, the blacksmithing and straw bag industries announced price increases. Qian Yingqiu Commits Suicide 133

Qian Yingqiu, a native of Suzhou, 39 years old, was an accountant at Lixing Tobacco Company at 1022 Wenjian Teacher Road. He suddenly committed suicide by poisoning himself behind others' backs at about 10:00 a.m. yesterday morning. Police Officer Dies in the Line of Duty, Police Station Holds Memorial Service 134

The straw rope shop opened by Zhu Guoshun, a native of Dongtai, at 187 Miaodong Road, Zhabei, was invaded and robbed by four bandits at about 7:30 p.m. on the 20th of last month, resulting in a loss of more than 20 yuan. According to the questioning by the Linping Road Police Station, a large number of officials were dispatched to search and arrest the bandits. The four bandits opened fire to resist arrest, causing patrol officer Xu Zhishun (No. 2711, a native of Ganyu, Jiangsu, 20 years old) to be shot in the left abdomen, breaking the large intestine and seriously injuring him. The four bandits escaped. Xu was sent to Tongren Hospital by car, but the treatment was ineffective, and he died at 8:00 a.m. the next day. The detailed process has been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the police station held a memorial service to show their condolences. More than 300 people from various branch bureaus, districts, teams, and public groups participated. The ceremony was performed as scheduled. First, Director Niu Jingjian reported the brief history of Xu's life and the process of his death. Feng Xiancheng, Yan Chengkuan, and Long Zhijian successively delivered speeches. After the ceremony, the entire team paraded to the wreaths and elegiac couplets sent by all sectors of society, which were mostly epigrams.

Five Bandits Captured in Nanshi and Sent for Trial, Rifles Found in Qibao Cemetery 135

Dong Mingde, the fifth team leader of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Brigade, and squad leader Liu Guangjun, based on a secret report from detective Gu Junqing, found that on the 1st of this month, a bandit tried to rob a municipal police officer's pistol in Panjia Lane in the city but failed. The two sides exchanged fire, and the bandits fled to Eddie Road and disappeared. On the 21st of this month, the violent bandits who robbed property from Ye Chengjun's house at 369 Penglai Road, Nanshi, were hiding in Room 17 of the Tonghai Inn in the Dongtingshan Lane of the Sixteen Puds of Nanshi, discussing going out to rob again. The situation was reported to Liu Huaiwai, the captain of the Detective Brigade, who immediately joined forces with the police chief of the jurisdiction and rushed to the scene at 10:00 p.m. The five violent bandits were captured on the spot. After questioning the team one by one, they confessed their names as Zhou Liufu, 33 years old, a native of Shishan; Chen Aqing, 32 years old, a native of Shandong; Li Yuetang, 41 years old, a native of Jiangwan; Yu Chunhe, 31 years old, a native of Gaoyou; and Zhu Miaogen, 26 years old, a native of Chongming. A 6-inch revolver was confiscated, with the inspection number 47817 and two bullets. They also confessed that there was another rifle and two rows of ten bullets stored in a grave in the countryside of Guanyintang, Qibao Town. The original handlers, together with the district police station, confiscated the rifle at 8:00 a.m. yesterday. It was stamped with the seal of the Songjiang County Government with the number 96, and another gun number was 2527. At the same time, the suspect Wang Baiqian, 28 years old, a native of Qibao, was also arrested. After questioning by the team, they were sent to the Public Security Bureau for trial along with the five bandits, weapons, and ammunition obtained earlier.

Resentment Over Business Competition, Piling Feces Case Sentenced, Wang Feng Paid Fine and Released 136

Feng Shaolan, a native of Changshu, opened Tongfaxiang Stone Powder Shop at 677 Yuqiaqing Road. His younger sister, Wang Feng, was married to Wang Yongfeng, a native of Suzhou who was in charge of the stone powder business at 7 Renzhili, Lane 156, North Zhejiang Road. Recently, Wang suffered from paralysis and could not preside over the work. Wang Feng took charge. The customers who had been dealing with Wang Yongfeng were suddenly taken away by Feng. Although she pleaded with him, Feng refused. She held a grudge in her heart and instigated the gangster Xu Youzhang to throw feces at Feng's head with feces on Xiamen Road on the 16th of the month, causing Feng to taste the yellow and white juice. Xu Youzhang was arrested and confessed to Wang Feng, so his father arrested her. The lawyer Xun Jiu from the first special district court prosecuted her for the crimes of injury and insult under criminal law. After questioning by Judge Ye Shengchao, Xu Youzhang and Wang Feng were sentenced to 15 days of detention each. If they were to commute the sentence with a fine, they would be allowed to convert it at the rate of two yuan per day. Wang Feng immediately raised cash, submitted it to the court, and was released.

Recently, flower association gambling in this city has revived. However, the arrests are strict, so those who collect gambling money are very secretive, so few are cracked. Yesterday evening at 5:00 p.m., Li Fuyi, the patrol chief of the Yimiao Police Station, was patrolling the Xinzha River area when he caught sight of an old man named Changgui (namely Xiao Changgui, 60 years old, a native of Taizhou, living at 1 Yangzhong Lane, Anren Street) running a flower association boat. Teenager Teased and Beaten, a Small Dispute 138

Zhou Shisheng, a local, used to work at the Tongxingchang Rope Factory in Liuliqiao, Pudong. His wife also worked at the factory. Xia Xinhou, the factory's bill collector, was only 18 years old, young and mischievous, and teased Zhou's wife, fabricating secrets and adding slander. The wife was very embarrassed and complained to her husband, Zhou Baosheng, who went to question Xia Xinhou, which caused a conflict. The weak teenager was no match for the strong man. His parents, Xia Xiaodi, 44 years old, and Xia Sun, 42 years old, heard that their son was bullied and rushed to the scene with a cane to beat Zhou Baosheng. Zhou Baosheng broke a rib. Zhou's wife reported the incident to the police, and Xia and his son were detained and sent to the local court. Zhou Baosheng was sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment and another injury doctor was hired to treat the fracture. Fortunately, he was out of danger. After Lei, the prosecutor, verified the injuries, the defendants were released on bail, and a public prosecution was filed against Xia and his son and wife for the crime of injury. Yesterday, Judge Chen opened the trial. The official said that the plaintiff's injuries had healed and that the matter was caused by a minor reason, so he asked both parties to go outside for reconciliation to settle the lawsuit. Both parties agreed, and the trial was adjourned to another date.

Suspicious Blood Flowing from Corpse, District Court Sends Personnel for Inspection 139

At about 3:00 p.m. yesterday, a car suddenly arrived at 151 Tiande Road, Zhabei, carrying a corpse covered in a cotton quilt with blood stains. The sentry found it and became suspicious. He went upstairs to investigate and found blood stains on the bed and pillow. He brought Shan Jiming, the second landlord of the house, to the police station for questioning. According to Shan's confession, his old friend Yu Rongsheng was unemployed and impoverished, and had no food or clothing. He had stayed at his house on the 8th of last month. Late at night the night before, Yu Rongsheng felt heartache and groaned frequently, then vomited blood non-stop until he died. Because Yu had no relatives, he hired a car to transport the body to the Tobacco Industry Association for coffin burial, and there was nothing hidden. The police station verified the confession, sent personnel to investigate and confirmed it to be true, released Shan, and ordered the local Jia to report to the local court to send a prosecutor to inspect the corpse on the scene for investigation.

Letter to the Editor 147

To the Editor, I recently read your newspaper's 21st [of December] report that the Shandong bandit Mao Jiwen was arrested in Shanghai based on a letter from the victim. After reading it, I was shocked and dismayed. I have been in Shanghai for many years, and I have been working as a teacher. My conduct has always been proper, but due to my straightforward nature and interactions with people, I fear that I may have been envied by petty people. The reason for being summoned by the police was actually due to a secret letter fabricated by malicious people. However, after examination, it has been proven that the scar on my leg is definitely not a gunshot wound, but was indeed caused by an unknown malignant sore in my childhood. Furthermore, with the guarantees of all parties, I am indeed a law-abiding civilian, and I was released immediately. The report in your newspaper has greatly affected my reputation. I hope that your newspaper will make corrections immediately. Respectfully, Mao Xiaowen of Shen Bao Guan Taiwan

Electrical Manufacturing Industry in Shanghai (Continued) 149

— Edited by China Credit Information

(No. 40 of Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview)

12. Kailang Dry Battery Factory—This factory is operated as a partnership by the three brothers Jiang Younan, Jiang Shaonan, and Jiang Bohou, with a small amount of outside investment. It was established in the 18th year of the Republic of China [1929]. Initially, it only manufactured batteries. Later, when the Yongfeng Hand-Held Lantern Shell Factory, which was run by their father Jiang Yinan, closed down the year before last, the factory also began to manufacture hand-held lantern shells. The total capital is 45,000 yuan. The factory base is located at No. 51, Sanyang Lane, West Baoxing Road, Zhabei, with more than a dozen rented rooms, divided into battery and lantern shell departments, employing more than 80 workers in total. The batteries produced by the factory are branded with the "Rongguang" trademark and can produce 1,000 dozen per day. The lantern shells can produce 50 to 100 dozen.

In addition to the above 12 companies, there are still many manufacturers of electrical materials such as light bulbs, batteries, and electric fans in this city. However, due to their average scale, they have little impact on the future of the industry, so they are not listed one by one.

3. Production and Sales of Electrical Materials

Current Situation

The sales of electrical materials produced by various factories are closely related to the season. For example, electric fans and irons are popular in the summer months, while electric stoves and hot pots are popular in the cold winter. Other items such as various flashlights also have better sales after the harvest, because people in the interior often have the purchasing power to purchase these items at that time. Currently, some manufacturers are working day and night to manufacture flashlights, precisely for this reason. In recent years, the sales of various military electrical materials have been particularly good, which is causally related to the rapid development of military transportation in recent years. As for the destinations of transportation, they vary depending on the type of electrical appliance. Generally speaking, flashlights are mainly sold in towns and cities north of the Yangtze River and along the Yangtze River where the electric lighting industry is not yet developed, and there are also considerable sales in Southeast Asia. Most of the batteries are transported to cities such as Hankou, Changsha, Chongqing, Yichang, Nanchang, and Anqing, and then resold to townships. This city and the Beijing-Hankou area mostly use foreign batteries. As for electric fans, electric stoves, irons, light bulbs, etc., only a few large cities can consume them, because the existence of the electrical industry is the only condition for their use. (To be continued)

Piece Goods A Glimpse of the Recent Woolen Fabric Market 154

The woolen fabric market can be described as excellent recently. Because the end of the year is approaching, and due to environmental factors, most holders are unwilling to extend credit. Buyers have no choice but to pay in cash, and business remains prosperous. After continuous investigation, the stock in this city seems to be in short supply. The import of Western goods from Europe and America has ceased, and what has been reported are completely thin goods for spring sales. Eastern goods have also arrived in small quantities, only postal deliveries. Domestic products cannot keep up. Ten-number riding breeches, Croton, horse-colored sleeve linings, etc., are all vying for fixed dyeing. The goods ordered ten days ago cannot be delivered one by one, resulting in Melton flat thick wool, various suit overcoat wool, riding breeches Croton, Coktin, long-haired camel fleece, horse-colored satin, French feet, silk feather yarn, women's colored wool, Qini, etc., all having a shortage of one yard for every yard sold. In the future, as the weather turns cold, the thick woolen fabric market will inevitably become more prosperous, causing the holders to remain optimistic and continue to look upwards. Unlike in previous years, overcoat wool fell in price after the festival. The foreign firms are said to be actively engaged in annual ordering business. Because people in the industry appreciate the current good market conditions, the shortage of goods, and high prices, many are adopting it. The collection of accounts has returned to one level. This year, the expectation is that the closing will be better than in previous years. The market this year has a sense of recovery and prosperity. The autumn harvest has been bountiful, and the woolen fabric and Western clothing shops, both large and small, can all expect profits. Therefore, accounts are easier to collect than in previous years.

Special Feature: Production, Sales, and Manufacturing of Keemun Black Tea 157

In the year 25 of the Republic of China (1936), the provinces of Anhui and Jiangxi, in an effort to revive their tea industries, initiated a unified sales plan. They also telegraphed the Ministry of Industries, requesting the dispatch of personnel to conduct origin inspections to prevent the proliferation of inferior teas. Consequently, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau sent personnel to expedite the preparations. This was completed in July, and a detailed report on the quality of tea products in the Keemun tea region was submitted. Now, amidst the accumulated problems of the tea industry, there is an urgent need for reorganization. Therefore, a portion of the report concerning production, manufacturing, and sales is excerpted and introduced to the readers. Editor's note: Keemun Black Tea is a general term for black tea produced in Keemun, Fuliang, Zhide, and Guichi. It is commonly referred to as "Keemun, Fuliang, and Zhide," omitting Guichi because of its relatively small tea production. Keemun Black Tea benefits from uniquely favorable natural conditions. Its color, aroma, and taste are not only leaders among domestic black teas but also enjoy a worldwide reputation in the international tea market. With high prices and broad sales, Keemun's production, despite having only over sixty years of history, has deeply impressed people both in China and abroad.

The production, manufacturing, and sales of Keemun Black Tea represent three different classes. Production is handled by tea farmers; refinement is done by tea firms; and sales are introduced to foreign firms by tea brokers. This year, the Anhui-Jiangxi Black Tea Unified Sales Office is taking over the role of tea brokers. As for foreign firms handling tea, they mostly act on behalf of overseas tea merchants, occupying the position of agents. Therefore, the ultimate responsibility for sales rests with overseas tea merchants. It should be noted that Keemun was not initially a producer of black tea. Sixty years ago, it was famous for producing green tea, which was transported and sold in Guangdong and Guangxi provinces and enjoyed a high reputation. Because its processing method was similar to that of Lu'an tea, it was also known as An tea. Until the second year of the Guangxu era (1876), a Mr. Yu from Yixian, who came from Zhide, established a workshop in Likou and encouraged tea farmers to manufacture black tea, purchasing it at high prices. This practice then spread to Shanli. Driven by profit, people switched to black tea production, leading to the world-renowned Keemun Black Tea of today. However, over the past sixty years, the production and sales of Keemun Black Tea have also gone from prosperity to decline, which should deeply alarm us.

(1) Production and Manufacturing of Keemun Black Tea

There have been no statistics on the exact area under tea cultivation in Keemun. Generally, tea plants are cultivated on fertile mountain slopes. Tea is also planted on plains. Tea farmers open up land on a small scale and it is scattered, making statistics impossible. According to estimates of tea production from the Department of Agricultural Economics of Jinling University, the total area of tea land in the Keemun region is over 81,500 mu.

Most tea farmers are self-cultivating. Unfortunately, there are no reliable statistics on the number of households. In addition to tea cultivation, tea farmers also grow other crops to supplement their income.

The production and manufacturing of Keemun Black Tea involve the tea farmers picking fresh leaves and producing rough tea. Tea farms are responsible for further processing and packaging into boxes. This division of labor completes the production and manufacturing of Keemun Black Tea.

In the past, the number of tea firms in the Keemun region was very small, with substantial capital. Some produced thousands of boxes of tea. Later, due to the high prices of tea, tea brokers competed to provide loans to secure tea boxes. As a result, the number of tea firms increased sharply, while the number of tea boxes produced decreased daily, and costs increased. This gradually led to crude manufacturing. From the number of tea firms and the number of tea boxes produced in Keemun over the years, we can understand the general situation.

Table of the Number of Tea Firms and the Number of Black Tea Boxes Produced in Keemun County Over the Years

The average number of tea boxes produced per tea firm in Keemun County was still 456 in 1928. By 1932, the number of tea firms had suddenly increased to 194, while the average number of tea boxes produced per firm had fallen to 205, a decrease of more than half compared to 1928. The reason for the sudden increase in the number of tea firms in that year was the exceptionally high price of tea in 1931, which led to speculative merchants setting up firms in large numbers to seek substantial profits. Subsequently, as tea prices declined year after year, the number of tea firms also tended to decrease. However, each firm still produced only about two hundred boxes of tea, so its manufacturing costs remained uneconomical.

The counties of Fuliang and Zhide have also exhibited the same trend. Tea production has decreased annually, while the number of tea firms has increased. In 1934, Fuliang had 63 tea firms producing 15,000 boxes of tea, averaging 238 boxes per firm. This year, the number of tea firms increased to 68, but tea production was only 17,876 boxes. Similarly, in Zhide, there were only 34 tea firms producing 10,000 boxes of tea in 1934. This year, the number of tea firms increased to 47, but produced only 11,045 boxes of tea. The number of tea firms and the output do not increase proportionally, resulting in an average decrease in the number of tea boxes produced by each firm. However, the expenses of all tea firms do not decrease proportionally with the number of tea boxes produced, resulting in higher costs for Keemun Black Tea.

Moreover, the widespread establishment of branch offices by tea firms to compete for rough tea is also one of the reasons for the increase in costs. In Keemun, in the southwest corner of the county, there is no need for 130 tea firms to engage in refinement; nor is there a need for each firm to widely establish branch offices to collect rough tea. This increases manufacturing costs and causes complications, while tea farmers gain no real benefits from rushing from one place to another. Sometimes, after repeated journeys, good quality rough tea undergoes excessive fermentation and deteriorates. Therefore, the large number of tea firms and the excessive establishment of branch offices hinder the development of Keemun Black Tea leaves.

Cooperative movements in the Keemun area began in Keemun in 1933, promoted and guided by the Keemun Tea Improvement Farm, pioneering tea farmers' cooperative tea production. At that time, with proper guidance, the results were significant. As a result, tea farmers followed suit and organized tea transportation, sales, and credit cooperatives to achieve the goals of self-production, self-manufacturing, and self-sales. The benefits of the cooperatives, in a passive sense, are sufficient to eliminate the exploitation of middlemen. In a positive sense, they are also sufficient to improve the living standards of tea farmers. The principles are pure, so they have been able to develop vigorously in three years. The number of cooperatives increased from only one in 1933 to 36 in 1936. The number of members also increased accordingly. The rapid development of cooperative movements in the past four years can be seen in the table below.

Table of the Number of Keemun Black Tea Production and Sales Cooperatives in the Past Four Years

The development of cooperative movements is indeed a positive phenomenon. However, to weigh the success of cooperative movements, quality is more important than quantity. If cooperatives can be well-organized and effective, tea farmers will join without being encouraged. Therefore, promoters of cooperative movements should not seek an increase in quantity but should prioritize quality. The future of cooperative movements is promising.

(2) The Trade of Keemun Black Tea

After Keemun Black Tea is refined and packaged into boxes, it is traditionally transported by water to Jiujiang and then transferred to Shanghai, where it is sold to foreign firms through tea brokers. This year, the authorities of Anhui and Jiangxi provinces implemented unified sales, changing to land transport to Shanghai. It is sold to various foreign firms by the Anhui-Jiangxi Black Tea Unified Sales Office without going through tea brokers. This is truly an unprecedented reform in the domestic trade of Keemun Black Tea in the past eighty years. Although the connection between tea brokers and inland tea firms has been interrupted, the power of foreign firms is still difficult to contain.

The largest purchaser of Keemun Black Tea is Jardine Matheson, a British trading company, accounting for two-fifths of Keemun's production. Other companies such as Gim Loong, Xiehe, Tianyu, Baochang, and Xingcheng also purchase significant amounts, followed by Huacha, Tongfu, and Tianxiang. According to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau's inspection statistics for the past four years, Jardine Matheson has exported the most Keemun tea each year, at 7,000 to 8,000 metric tons per year. Other foreign firms export a few dozen metric tons at the low end, and only 3,000 to 4,000 metric tons at the high end. A comprehensive review of the table below will reveal the Keemun tea trade situation of various trading companies.

Table of the Quantity of Keemun Black Tea Exported by Major Tea Exporters in the Past Four Years (Unit: Metric Tons)

Summary of Methods for Improving Agricultural Crops 158

— Gu Fu

The goal of improving agricultural crops is nothing more than increasing yield and improving quality, and its ultimate goal is to increase revenue. We advocate that research on yield and quality should not only use statistical methods to compare the results, but also recognize that yield and quality are composed of many factors. We should work on factor analysis, and try to describe the main items as follows:

1. Cellular aspects, such as the number of chromosomes and their genome situation.

2. Morphological aspects, such as the depth and distribution of roots, the amount of tillering or branching, and the condition of fruiting.

3. Physiological aspects, such as the earliness or lateness of maturity, and the strength or weakness of fertilizer tolerance.

4. Ecological aspects

A. The impact on the environment, such as drought resistance and cold resistance.

B. The relationship with diseases and insects. According to the type of crop, select the main diseases and insect pests, and investigate the resistance capacity.

The above items are all related to yield and quality, and they are also interconnected, making it difficult to make accurate judgments. Therefore, they are analyzed into two categories: normal and abnormal. Taking yield as an example, under normal conditions, it can be estimated from cellular, morphological, and physiological aspects. Under abnormal conditions, it can be estimated from ecological relationships, so there are slight clues to follow. Furthermore, the characteristics of each variety are partly hereditary and partly adapted to the environment. Hereditary traits do not undergo mutations under normal conditions, making them more reliable and easier to study. Environmental adaptations change at any time and place, making them extremely complex and requiring cultivation in various environments before they can be understood, making research more difficult. Studying them separately will provide more clues.

However, hereditary traits are also based on the principle of survival of the fittest. The varieties preserved today must have traits suitable for the production environment. Because the climate, topography, water conservancy, and soil quality vary from place to place, the types and varieties of crops suitable for them also vary. If we want to improve agricultural crops, we should first investigate the conditions in various places, divide them into regions, and generally specify which types of varieties are suitable for a certain region and which cultivation methods should be applied. When breeding, these types of varieties should be used as basic varieties to begin with. Taking Jiangsu rice as an example, the area north of the Yangtze River is an early indica rice area, the Jingzhen area is a mid-indica rice area, the Su-Chang area is a late japonica rice area, the area near Yutan is a glutinous rice area, and Pudong is an early japonica rice area. Once the regions are divided, the varieties suitable for each region are also limited.

Once the area for a certain type of crop has been defined, investigate the original varieties in the area and select the one that is planted most widely in the area and has the highest yield over the years to serve as the basic variety. Perform selection or crossbreeding within this basic variety. Strive to save labor in breeding, shorten the number of years, and ensure that the results are reliable.

We advocate that when carrying out breeding, it is very important to first delineate regions and limit varieties. As for the breeding work itself, it is considered less important. In terms of pure line breeding, limiting the selection of panicles or plants in the first year will prevent the number of selected lines from being too large. In areas with large regions and many varieties, select two to three thousand, such as late japonica rice in Jiangnan. In areas with small regions and few varieties, selecting only a few hundred is sufficient. However, the selection area should not be biased towards one corner but should be spread throughout the region. In the first year, there should also be single-panicle rows or single-plant rows, but the selection criteria should not be based on visual observation and comparison with control rows to determine whether to take or discard. Each row should be sown with one grain or planted with a single plant to facilitate the investigation of its various characteristics. Before carrying out breeding, it is necessary to determine the goal. In addition to increasing yield per mu, attention should also be paid to one or several of the following aspects based on local conditions: earliness, drought resistance, disease resistance, and insect resistance. Then the selection goal can also be defined. In the second and third years, the number of repetitions and the amount of seeds are gradually increased. The row system is still used, and the selection goal, in addition to paying attention to the investigation of various growth traits, also measures yield. After the fourth year, a small-scale system can be adopted, with the size of each area tentatively set at one-twentieth of a mu, repeated three times, and continued for three years. The block arrangement method is used to eliminate differences in soil and years using variance analysis, accurately identifying the high or low yield of the lines. The characteristics that require a large amount of data can also be checked after the fourth year. Select the excellent ones and carry out propagation.

Starting from the seventh year, in addition to distributing them to agricultural farms in various counties in the region to conduct regional trials, they should also be planted in various different environments to observe their adaptability. For example, rice should be applied with a large amount of fertilizer or a small amount of fertilizer to test its fertilizer tolerance and determine whether it is suitable for fertile or barren land, and whether it requires a large amount of fertilizer or only a small amount of fertilizer. Various depths of water should also be irrigated to test its suitability for dry land or wet land, terraced fields, flat fields, or polder fields. After clearly investigating the impact of the environment on each line, it can be decided which type of land is suitable for the species and which cultivation method should be used.

At this time, various cultivation methods can be applied according to the characteristics of each line to regulate it. For example, if the tillering of rice is small, the planting density should be increased to increase the number of individuals, thereby compensating for the reduction in the number of tillers per individual, so that the yield per unit area is not reduced. Ensure that the cultivation methods used are exactly what the line needs to maximize production.

Regarding crossbreeding methods, the Japanese system can be followed, dividing the country into several regions based on climate, topography, water conservancy, and soil quality. Each region should have a national agricultural experiment branch to carry out large-scale crossbreeding work until F3. Then, these seeds should be distributed to the provincial agricultural experiment stations in the region to continue cultivation, conduct rigorous investigations, and gradually eliminate them until F7. Then, they should be distributed to the county-level agricultural experiment stations in the province to cultivate them until the crossbred species is fixed.

Therefore, we also have special insights into the organization of agricultural crop improvement agencies and their business. It is believed that the main task of the central agricultural crop improvement agency is to conduct research on various methods, such as testing the flour milling rate of wheat, which equipment to use, and investigating the drought resistance of rice, which methods to use. After obtaining considerable results through precise research, publish them to the public so that the experiment stations in various places can use them. As for the agricultural crop improvement agencies in each province, they should be divided into several regions according to the climate, topography, water conservancy, soil quality, and people's habits in the province. Each region should establish an agricultural crop experiment station to preside over breeding, cultivation method experiments, etc. Taking Jiangsu as an example, Xuhai is a miscellaneous grain area, the coastal area is a cotton area, Jiangnan is a late japonica rice area, and Huainan is an early indica rice area. A provincial experiment station should be established in each area to handle it. If the central agency focuses on breeding work, although the equipment is complete and the talents are gathered, the improved varieties bred may only be suitable for the local climate and soil conditions, and cannot be popularized throughout the country. The talents and equipment cannot be used to their full potential and achieve the greatest effect. It is also inappropriate for each province not to divide regions by crop type. For example, if the Jiangsu wheat experiment station is located in Tongshan, it cannot take care of the wheat crop improvement in Jiangnan. If the rice crop experiment station is located in Songjiang, it does not focus on wheat crops, so that Wujin, Wuxi, and Yixing, the main wheat-producing areas, have no provincial agency to take responsibility for improvement. The provincial agricultural crop experiment stations in each region of a province and the county-level agricultural experiment stations should be interconnected and cooperate thoroughly, like the arm uses the finger, and the finger uses the arm. In this way, adapt to the local conditions, divide the work, and cooperate to study the excellent varieties and cultivation methods suitable for each place. In this way, the improvement of agricultural crops can be expected soon.

Mr. Gu Zhenji sent me a private discussion on improving agricultural crop methods written by him. It has been accumulated for more than 20 years of experience. The content of this work is known to be precise and detailed. I always think that to solve the current problem of people's food, the negative way is to adjust, and the positive way is to increase production. Nowadays, many wise people are more inclined to adjustment. It is understood that the effect of increasing production is slower and the matter is more complicated. However, increasing production must start with improving crops, and those who can regard this as a lifelong career and are tireless are rare, as far as I know, like Mr. Gu. Therefore, I chose a section from the full text, "Summary of Methods for Improving Agricultural Crops" for publication, to see a glimpse, so that you can know the path of agricultural crop improvement. (Liutang)
