Please Let Sisters Across the Country Accomplish This Wonderful Deed 159

— Juanhua

Dear Sisters,

For the past few years, we have always believed that only by implementing armed resistance can we save our country from danger.

Now, the battle drums of Eastern Sui have sounded. The enemy, insatiable in their greed, has launched a large-scale offensive against Suiyuan. Our soldiers, defending our land, are resolutely resisting regardless of the cost, which is something all the people of our country should wholeheartedly support. Good news is coming one after another. The Bailing Temple and the Great Temple have been successively recovered by our army. If this continues, the lost territories of the past, as long as the whole country is united, will not be difficult to recover in due course within a reasonable period of time, wiping out the extraordinary shame and humiliation of the past. However, this task is by no means something that a few people can accomplish. It must be realized by all our compatriots, contributing strength and money, under the common goal of resisting the enemy.

Recently, the amount of donations from various places to support Suiyuan is also quite a lot, but to demand long-term resistance, a large amount of supply is necessary. I now have a small suggestion to be adopted by sisters all over the country. The method is very simple: save your daily cosmetics money to help the soldiers defending the land in the front, because it doesn't matter if we don't use cosmetics for a day.

Friends, don't take it as a joke. At first glance, it seems like a drop in the bucket and won't help, but as long as you gather the strength of the majority, you may be able to build a tower from sand and make a small contribution to the country. Assuming that there are 40 million sisters in the country who use cosmetics (this is the minimum number), if they save it in one day, at least each person can save five cents (sisters in the city must save more than this amount), then a total of two million yuan can be saved. This is a considerable sum of money. If this money is remitted to the front, how meaningful and practical it will be, and how glorious it will be for our women's community! This is an easy task and there is no difficulty in doing it. I hope that female compatriots all over the country will practice it. In particular, I would like to ask the sisters in schools to take the lead in promoting and completing this meaningful good deed. (Editor's note: It is best to ask a bank in Shanghai to collect this donation specifically. Once a considerable amount is collected, it will be remitted to the front to see how much results can be achieved.)

A Brief Review of "Extraordinary Woman Assassins Yin" 160

— Ding Xiaoru

Together with the Shi Jianqiao assassination of Sun case, it is a heroic act. It can give female compatriots a lift! Dying for one's country, she can be called a female hero! Yin, the Deputy Official who died with her, cannot be "mentioned in the same breath".

The country has been brought to such a critical point, if there are still heartless people who are willing to betray and act as accomplices to tigers, how shameful and punishable is that? There is an ancient saying that goes, "Rebellious officials and traitors, everyone has the right to punish them!"

Whenever there is a great turbulent era, many extraordinary people and events are produced. Recently, there has been a news story in the newspaper entitled "Record of Extraordinary Woman Assassin Yin". The traitor Yin willingly acted as a traitor, and has long been reviled by the people of the country! Now there is actually such an extraordinary woman who went to plot an assassination, and the result was that she sacrificed a precious life in vain. No one who has read it does not applaud and sigh! What's more, risking an assassination is not as harmless and convenient as acting in a play?

We only need to see her meticulous design, and for the sake of the great righteousness of the country and the nation, she can disregard everything and sacrifice herself. It can be said that she is both wise and brave! And after the failure, she was subjected to brutal torture by × Fang to force a confession, but she was still calm and fearless, and cursed at Yin until death without saying who was instigating her, which is even more awe-inspiring and admirable!

Although her result was unfortunately a failure, she died for her country. But her spirit is eternal; her death can be said to be great, glorious, and even more sufficient to show the evil of Yin's betrayal.

There was also a man named Yin who died with her - Yin's deputy official. Although he also died for conspiring to assassinate without success, his initial motivation was because he could gain both money and beauty. Moreover, he was originally an traitor. The cause of the failure was rooted in his inability to keep secrets. He did not not know that his mother was the traitor's wet nurse, although it was safe to move her away, why did he have to tell her the secret plot of the assassination? If this is said to be filial piety, it is too foolish! As a result, the good thing was destroyed and it can be said to be "a child cannot be entrusted with great things". In addition, the old woman did not understand the great righteousness, but only knew to value her personal kindness, and secretly told Yin in advance, hoping to take the opportunity to claim credit and still protect her son. Who thought it was still in vain! This is simply even more foolish! Therefore, her extinction is the result of "asking for it". Her son's death is also not to be regretted and absolutely cannot be compared with that extraordinary woman. (This is the truth, and the author's words are not biased.)

It is said that the extraordinary woman used to be a dancer and was also someone's concubine. But her past status cannot cause her present reputation to suffer any loss. It is precisely because of this that it is even more commendable! Because the lives of ordinary dancers and concubines are mostly romantic and spoiled. It is difficult to say that such a touching, earth-shattering event can be done by non-dancers and concubines. Even among educated intellectuals, there are few people with this kind of courage! This is why it is so extraordinary. If we compare Yin with those men who are still drunk, dreaming, and indulge in singing and dancing, we should truly be ashamed!

Nowadays, ordinary playwrights in Shanghai often put some startling "social news" on the stage. I think it's okay to adapt the story of this extraordinary woman into a script. If it is performed, the content will be full of twists and turns, and it will definitely move the audience! Originally, using the art of drama to promote the "save the country" movement is a "very meaningful" and "effective" method. After watching this story, people can be awakened and strive to know that the "popular will of China is not dead", and the vitality is still "vigorous"! At the same time, it can be understood that Chinese women are not completely "weak and incompetent" people!

Northeastern Women Surviving Winter 161

— Xue Wen

The weather outside the Great Wall in winter is so cold, it's deadly cold. All day long, harsh, face-stinging north winds blow, and the ground is often covered with deep snow. There are far fewer people walking on the streets, and everywhere is filled with a desolate atmosphere.

The women of the Northeast, especially those in rural areas, have long been known for their ability to endure hardship and work hard. They work in the fields just like men. But in winter, because of the cold weather, they certainly can't work outdoors anymore. However, this doesn't mean they're idle; in fact, they're busy working all day long.

The first thing is sewing clothes and quilts. Because ordinary families all need to prepare new cotton clothes or take apart and wash old quilts in the late autumn and early winter for winter protection against the cold. Although this is not too heavy a task, putting a family's clothing together means they have to be busy for a considerable length of time. Therefore, every winter, because the days are short, they always light the lamps every night to do needlework, and only go to bed late at night.

However, what about the morning? They still get up especially early. The cold weather often causes their hands to freeze and crack, even to the point of bleeding. After eating breakfast, they are still busy with needlework.

Because it's cold, they have to put a brazier or stove in the room to keep it relatively warm, so in addition to other proper work, they also have to be careful about this kind of thing.

In addition, because the weather is unpredictable, you can't say when it will snow, so whenever they see the weather turning cloudy, they have to quickly tidy up the firewood pile and prepare firewood for several days. The north wind scraping their faces is as uncomfortable as a knife cutting, which is really painful. However, they have to do it, because if it snows, wet firewood cannot be burned immediately.

In addition, in some places, women are required to carry water, so they have to endure the cold and climb the slippery well platform covered with thick ice. That's an even more difficult job.

The Transformation of Russian Women in the Past Twenty-Five Years 162

— Hua Ling

Mrs. Hooterow, a reporter for the American New Era magazine, traveled to Russia in 1912. Recently, she returned for a three-week stay. After returning to the United States, she wrote an article, "Russian Women in the Past Twenty-Five Years," which compares women in the old Russian era with women in the new Russian era, which is extremely interesting. She said that when she traveled to Russia before the Great War, she stayed for two months. The Russian women she came into contact with could be classified into levels. The first level was aristocratic women. They did not have the melancholy mood that Russians possess. They spent all day long laughing and giggling, holding concerts, dancing, watching plays, and paying attention to clothing and decoration. This was their daily work. The second class was housewives in ordinary families. Although they did not have the economic strength of aristocratic women, they also had to try their best to live their extravagant and enjoyable vain lives. Although they were often scolded, and even beaten, by their husbands because of this, few were willing to change their outwardly strong but inwardly weak lives. The last type was the poor women, who accounted for more than 70%. Relying on simple family industrial income, or serving as slaves in aristocratic families, or even relying on secret prostitution or begging, they helped their husbands support the family or maintain their own lives. At least half of the children born to these poor women became homeless children because they were really unable to raise them. But on this trip to Russia, traces of these three classes could not be found. In a town more than 140 miles from Moscow, she met a mayor's wife, an elementary school principal, and several female workers in a public canteen. The mayor's wife was a local female doctor who also knew a little English. Mrs. Hu only knew that she was the mayor's wife after talking to her for a while, because her clothes were as simple as those of rural women in the western United States, and she only ate black bread and two dishes with soup like other diners. No one could tell her status. According to the mayor's wife, women in Soviet Russia, like men, only know how to work and do not know how to enjoy extravagance and idleness. As she spoke, she raised her feet for Mrs. Hu to see. It turned out that the flat leather shoes she was wearing were only worth one dollar a pair in the United States and were worn by black women. There was also a patch half an inch in diameter on her left shoe.

Mrs. Hu said that before coming to Russia, she heard people say that there were a surprisingly large number of homeless children in Soviet Russia because it was too easy for couples to divorce, and after the divorce, no one was responsible for raising children. But on this trip to Russia, she realized that the story needed to be compared, because when she traveled to Russia in 1912, she rarely saw the footprints of homeless children in the bustling streets, because at that time, the police in the bustling streets ruthlessly beat homeless children with batons. The birthplace of these children was, in fact, poor families, so when you stepped into the slums, you would often be surrounded by dozens of homeless children, who would even rob you of your jewelry and handbags. At that time, it was said that there were more than 200,000 homeless children in St. Petersburg alone, and there were homeless children all over the country. But now, it is said that there are less than 100,000 homeless children in the entire city of Moscow. Although this official report cannot be completely believed, it is a fact that there are fewer homeless children now than in the past. Moreover, this situation is not limited to Moscow. The situation was exactly the same in the places she passed through during her trip to Russia, which was more than one thousand seven hundred miles.

Twenty-five years ago, when Mrs. Hu traveled to Russia, less than 5% of the poor women, who accounted for more than 70%, had received three or four years of education and knew a few words. This was still the situation in St. Petersburg. In rural areas, it can be said that less than one or two in a hundred. But on this same trip, in the streetcars, you could see female workers reading books or newspapers everywhere. It is said that in Soviet Russia, 57.75% of women under the age of 40 are literate. Although women over the age of 40 do not know Russian, they can read books and newspapers in Latin pinyin and write in Latin pinyin. It has also accounted for more than 70%. In today's Russia, there is one thing that is completely different from American women. The more knowledgeable American women are, the more addicted they are to luxury and enjoyment. Soviet Russian women, on the other hand, the more knowledgeable they are, the harder they work, and the simpler their lives become. This is an important transformation of Soviet Russian women in the past twenty-five years that cannot be ignored. On this trip to Russia, Mrs. Hu had some contact with some knowledgeable women and asked them, "The first five-year plan has been completed, and now the restrictions on people's clothing, food, and drink are not as strict as before. So, why don't you wear fashionable clothes and put on lipstick?" A small part of their answers was that it had become a habit, but a large part was that "there are no more prostitutes in Soviet Russia who use beauty to lure people."

Wild Child 164

— Man Zi

Wild children are looked down upon, because although they are also lovely, innocent, and naturally uninhibited little angels, they have not been recognized by the family for their status and position, and cannot inherit the great lineage, so they become fatherless children. But in a certain period, they will also be valued, because the ancestral lineage law, which cannot be without an heir, compels them to find an heir through exhaustive thinking, and then the wild child becomes a family child.

The facts tell us that in many large families, wild children have become the sons who carry on the lineage, and in many large families, wild children have been abandoned, leaving them to drift and have no one to rely on. This is all dominated by feudal forces. The fortune and misfortune of wild children is indeed a matter of the entire family system, and the mothers of wild children have even more tragic encounters. "Keeping the pearl and discarding the casket" is the most common means. Even if both the pearl and the casket are kept, there is not much good fortune. As for the mother becoming noble because of her son, it is really rare.

The new film "Qingming Season" features a wild child, which constitutes many tortuous plots. The darkness of society and the corruption of the family are contrasted from the negative side; the sense of justice of sympathetic people and the true love of human nature are highlighted from the positive side. A wild child who is valued by Zhao Meng and despised by Zhao Meng is turned upside down, especially the mother of the wild child, who is truly in a situation where she doesn't know whether to laugh or cry. Li Minghui speaks on behalf of many weak women who have been tempted, trampled on, and abandoned in "Qingming Season", and Shen Jun calls for many wild children who have been manipulated and dominated. After watching this, we feel whether the ancestral lineage law can exist? And how should the current law protect wild children? These are all issues that need to be discussed. In history, we can also see several wild children who have done earth-shattering great things and made bright and splendid great contributions. However, what kind of treatment should the government give to the education and sanitation of wild children? What kind of reasonable attitude should society have towards wild children? These are all the answers that "Qingming Season" asks of the audience.

The Great Disturbance That Shook the Students Studying in Japan 166

— Ying Zi

Pei Manna was slandered for no reason and used all her strength to fight back; Wei Jin pretended to be mentally ill in an attempt to evade responsibility.

(Tokyo Communication) Ms. Pei Manna is from Quan County, Guangxi. After graduating from Shanghai Art University, she returned to her province to work for two years and served as a teacher at Nanning Provincial Third Girls' Middle School. She came to Japan to study two years ago and is currently studying in the Department of Social Sciences at Tokyo Hosei University.

Her family is not very well-off. Her father passed away early, and she and her younger brother were raised by her great mother through hard work. Therefore, her past life was miserable and difficult. It cannot be said that she has achieved today's achievements without her own efforts and hard work. Due to continuous training and life's tribulations, she has been forged into a tough character.

Her current life is very simple. In addition to attending classes, she stays in the dormitory and reads the books she has planned. Her room is filled with newspapers and magazines, and there have never been cosmetics on the table. She doesn't put on lipstick, doesn't apply powder, and doesn't like to dress up. She has completely shed the typical image of a woman and walks strongly and boldly, and is known as a female soldier. She is sincere and loyal to her friends, has a very clear understanding of society, is not accustomed to family and enjoyable life, is quiet in nature, but also likes to debate with friends or explore various issues, and also participates in group activities when she is free. When she plays, she is very willful. But when she starts working, she becomes strict and serious, especially when it comes to the feudal forces that oppress women and all the old ethics and traditional concepts that despise women, she spares no effort in criticizing them, and she is brave in doing things. As long as she thinks it is beneficial to society, she does it regardless of everything!

She is still young, but she has grasped the correct reason and is moving forward. She often encourages her friends: "The cause of life depends entirely on one's own struggle. As long as a person does not covet vanity, does not rely on others, and is determined to endure hardship, take risks, and constantly hone himself, he will eventually achieve his goal." In this way, her future is very promising.

The following is a conversation I had with her. She has recently been busy dealing with a leaflet that was distributed under a false name to insult her. This incident has caused a sensation in the Tokyo student community and has greatly affected the reputation of female students. Therefore, I visited her about this recently-occurring practical problem.

"What is the truth about the leaflet incident that happened recently? Please give your opinion."

"Ah! Mentioning this matter is embarrassing for me. To be honest, it would be easier for people to believe if it were said by a third party, but it seems not very good to speak if it happens to be the person involved. However, on the other hand, the truth of the matter is only clear to the parties involved. It is very reasonable to disclose the matter truthfully without exaggeration and to analyze it from an objective perspective. This incident has been going on for a month (and is still evolving), providing a lot of information to students studying in Tokyo and giving great stimulation to female students, but there are too few people who understand the truth and use correct criticism. I am excited that you are asking me about this issue today, and I am willing to tell you and my sisters in China from a third-party perspective.

This incident looks like a boring act on the surface, and can be dismissed, but if we recognize it strictly, it can also be regarded as a major problem. If we are satisfied with ignoring it, I am afraid that the victims will follow one after another, because the bankruptcy of reputation is enough to kill people and cut off their paths. Like the past "Ruan Lingyu", she lost her life only because "gossip is a fearful thing". For example, a female student Wang in Tokyo was slandered by a leaflet distributed because she did not accept the love of a man named Chen. Even now, some people still call her an concubine. This is obviously a man's excessive selfishness and intentional fabrication and slander. For example, recently Xiong was also distributed a leaflet with no facts because she did not accept a man's request. She could not bear this poisonous harm, and as a result, she passively ran back to her hometown. This not only fails to get people's sympathy, but also helps the evildoer by saying that she fled in fear of crime. Then, are real women so easily bullied? Are they going to be ruined one by one by that kind of unfounded leaflet?

Speaking of the cause of my leaflet, it is like this: Last year, my fellow villager "Zeng Yi" divorced "Wei Jin" (the divorce notice was published in the Tokyo Student News). Because I have a deeper relationship with her, and said a few fair words in the final negotiations, I was therefore poisoned and hated by him. For a year, he gave me a lot of slander and attacks. I have always ignored it for the sake of peace. However, things happened unexpectedly. He actually went too far and actually committed the crime of borrowing someone else's name."

"Please briefly describe the process of their divorce and the content of this leaflet."

"Speaking of their divorce, it was inevitable, because if the two people cannot love each other, then of course it is better to separate. But the man turned love into hate and forced her to commit suicide twice, wanting her to swallow gold. This can be seen from this. Speaking of the act of distributing leaflets, he first committed the crime of killing people with a borrowed knife. He openly used the name of a third party, Zhao Wenyuan (according to Zhao, Mr. Zeng Tu's friend Wei Jin often regarded him as a rival in love), to print and distribute it, and the wording was extremely fabricated and insulting, such as "introducing boyfriends", "cheating money", and "forging diplomas". Chen Supervisor was also involved in this, because Chen Supervisor also reprimanded him when they divorced. In short, Wei Jin's actions regarded women's reputation as a child's play, only seeking his own happiness, regardless of destroying others. Such a student who bears the heavy responsibility of the country is really heartbroken!"

"Now that things have reached this point, how are you going to deal with it? Has the student supervision office and the women's association responded concretely?"

"After this incident happened, I submitted a letter to our country's official office in Japan, requesting a thorough investigation and strict punishment, and I have already published a statement in the newspaper. The Women's Association and the Hometown Association have also unanimously provided assistance. - According to a friend close to Wei Jin, he is now pretending to be mentally ill in an attempt to evade responsibility, and has been admitted to the hospital for treatment. In this way, friends have expressed sympathy and secretly advised me to forgive him, but now I regard this issue as my own issue, and the main thing is to eradicate the erroneous thinking and the false behavior, and give a head-on blow to the general public who have impure views on women. Men sometimes look for entertainment or vent their anger, but women are greatly affected, or even their entire future will be ruined because of this. It is really chilling... So I am determined to use all my strength to fight and achieve my goal by standing on the interests of women as a whole and protecting the reputation of female students studying in Tokyo. I hope to eradicate this kind of behavior and give Wei Jin a severe punishment so that students studying in Tokyo will not have this kind of behavior again in the future. I hope that everyone will clarify the truth and maintain justice. If I can get my wish, this will not only be Manna's personal fortune, but also a great fortune for all female students studying in Tokyo."

Is it a Human? Is it a Beast? 167

— Snow Shadow

Qi Shi, barely seven years old, already donned her second set of mourning clothes, transforming from an orphan into a sorrowful orphan. Such a frail little girl, having lost both her father and mother, how could she possibly continue to live? In this world where humans and beasts are indistinguishable!

Fortunately, Qi Shi's grandfather didn't follow his son and daughter-in-law, and he so lovingly doted on this little granddaughter, not disliking her in the least because she was a girl. Although he was a poor scholar, over sixty and already aging, his home lacking even the most basic three thatched huts, he was fortunate enough, due to his long-standing poverty, to still hold a clerical position at an inland shipping company, earning thirty-two yuan in legal tender each month. He had joined this company at the age of thirty-five, working there for twenty-seven years, receiving only two salary increases, two yuan each time. He didn't resent his boss; he felt that with society in such a depressed state, having someone willing to provide a meal was already good. When his son was alive, he had enjoyed about seven years of great happiness, with the family's living expenses entirely borne by Ya Zi, his own earnings only needed for his personal expenses. Unexpectedly, his son suddenly died, and the small savings he left behind were only enough to cover his funeral expenses. In less than a year, his daughter-in-law also died, emptying the old man's savings accumulated over the years. Although deeply saddened, he didn't despair. He self-sufficiently raised his granddaughter, continuing to diligently perform his work.

Qi Bao was already studying at a small private school nearby. Although it was less than two hundred steps from home, her grandfather always personally escorted her three times a day: to school in the morning, home at noon, and back to school in the afternoon. Only for the afternoon dismissal, as he couldn't leave the company, he entrusted her to a young mistress living in the same residence. Qi Bao's liveliness and loveliness, as well as her grandfather's kindness and gentleness, were praised by almost everyone on their street. If a person still had a human heart, no matter how much they enjoyed causing trouble, they would never target this grandfather and granddaughter.

One windy afternoon, Qi Bao waited a long time at the school gate, but couldn't see the white-haired old man. Her little stomach was so hungry she couldn't bear it any longer, so she risked running home alone. But her grandfather wasn't home either, only Zhang Ma, the cook, waiting anxiously at the gate. Qi Bao, hearing that her grandfather hadn't returned, didn't want to eat and insisted that Zhang Ma take her to the inland shipping company.

"Look at a madman, look at a madman!" At the gate of the shipping company, a crowd of people gathered, surrounding an old man gesturing wildly and cursing loudly. His face had turned ashen, his old eyes wide open, but the eyeballs had turned red, and white foam was dripping from the corners of his mouth, truly resembling a madman.

"You bone-gnawing beasts! Have you no regard for twenty-seven years of loyalty!"

"Old! Old! Old! How could your father get old? Beasts! You've drained all my energy! Youth, middle age, from black hair I've worked for you until my hair turned white, all my useful energy exhausted, and now you嫌 me for being old!" He stretched his hoarse voice and shouted, tears rolling down his beard like drops of dew. He pointed his finger at the gloomy building, wishing he could pierce through it and point directly at the faces of the people inside. "You beasts! You can't even bear to give me this one mouthful of food! You're so heartless!… You have money to take concubines and send your sons to Japan; can't you spare me these few coins? You heartless beasts!…"

Those who initially thought he was crazy, hearing his coherent words, realized he was a discarded old employee. But who could stand up for him and speak out against the injustice?

"Daddy! Did a beast bite you? Where is the beast?" Qi Bao always thought some beast had truly bitten her grandfather, so she rushed forward, stretched out her little hands, and hugged him tightly.

"Where is the beast? Isn't it inside the building?" Her grandfather's hand was still pointing towards the building.

"Those inside the building are people!" Qi Bao asked doubtfully.

"They are beasts! They are beasts!…"

Cessation of Menstruation

She took several bottles of "Dang Gui Er" a month ago, but it hasn't been effective. Now I have several questions, so please answer them: (1) What medicine can make menstruation accurate and replenish weakness? Can "Dang Gui Er" continue to be taken? (2) Will this disease turn into consumption of dried blood? If it does, what medicine can cure it? (4) Is there any danger? (5) Can it be cured in a short period? (6) Is there hope for childbirth?

Coughing and Night Sweats

No. 136, No. 793, Suzhou Road, Shanghai, Mr. Cao Kai asks: Respectfully, my eldest son is thirteen years old and has a weak constitution. Every winter, he has a cough, although not severe, it is not easily completely cured; and every night his head has hot sweats that wet the pillow, this has been the case every winter for three years. Since contracting malaria in mid-October this year, although he recovered after three weeks, his left scrotum suddenly became swollen – to a length of more than two inches – and there was a slight pain. It shrinks to its original shape after sleeping at night, but it still feels painful when shaken, and it is still swollen after getting up in the morning. It has been almost a month, and although he has taken hernia pills, it has not been effective. The pain has now been reduced, but due to the swelling, walking is very inconvenient. May I ask: (1) What medicine should be taken for a weak cough? (2) What causes the nighttime head sweats? What medicine can cure it? (3) Is the scrotal swelling a hernia? What medicine is most effective? Is it necessary to seek a face-to-face consultation? Because I am currently in the countryside, coming to Shanghai is very inconvenient.

Answer: (1) There is a suspicion of lung "tuberculosis", take "Cod Liver Oil 'Star Brand'" "Pills Creobote" (2) Night sweats are a symptom of tuberculosis, take "Ecid Camphoric", and apply all methods of recuperation for tuberculosis! (3) It is a hernia, undergo surgical treatment, medication is ineffective. (4) It is not necessary to ask for my consultation, consult a formal doctor locally.

(2) Yes, it is called "liver syphilis", but the process is not so fast. If the course of syphilitic liver disease is as fast as described in the letter, it is nothing but "syphilitic liver cirrhosis".

Gossip

The End of the Road for Traitors 168

— Meng Ruo

Selling one's country for personal glory is the sole ambition of a traitor. Selling the country allows them to hold high positions and enjoy generous salaries. This is indeed considered a shrewd move. Therefore, many unscrupulous individuals disregard the enormity of their crimes, ignoring the curses hurled at them, and persist in their treachery. However, while some have succeeded in achieving personal glory through betrayal, as evidenced by the current batch of puppet officials, big and small, who have risen to prominence, and the arch-traitor Yin, who dominates his own territory as a puppet leader, many others have faced unfortunate circumstances, leading them to a dead end. The number one traitor, Zheng Xiaoxu, once enjoyed a period of得意, but now he has faded into obscurity. He himself never imagined that his old age would be so desolate. As for others who have been kicked away by their masters, they are naturally even more pitiful.

Take, for example, the bandit-Mongolian puppet troops who recently launched a large-scale invasion of Suiyuan. Wang Ying, this rebel, certainly harbored grand dreams of selling his country for personal glory. But what was the outcome? According to Guihua Telegraph: "After the failure of the Wang Ying bandits, they fled with their remnants to the Shimuerte area. Recently, under the orders of a certain party, they were transferred from Shimuerte to Jiabi Temple north of Shangdu. The certain party ordered him to lead several hundred remnants to harass western Suiyuan. Wang requested additional firearms, but the certain party refused. Wang was greatly dissatisfied. Fearing that Wang would defect, the certain party assassinated Wang at the temple on the twenty-first night, and Wang's remnants were immediately disarmed."

Since the outbreak of the Suiyuan War, there have been rumors that Wang himself intended to defect. If Wang could have realized his errors early on and led his troops to surrender, he might have been able to wash away the stain of treason. However, blinded by greed, he continued to resist stubbornly, inevitably leading him to his demise. This can be considered a form of retribution for his heinous crimes. Those who hope to taste the rewards of treason should take this as a warning.

The Night Watchman 169

— Fan Jia

These past few nights, I've been hearing the sound of the night watchman again. In the stillness of the cold night air, the sounds of the gong and clapper are clear and steady, as if the watchman's憂鬱 is vented through that copper gong and clapper. I don't like sleeping with my head covered by the blankets, even in winter; but when I hear the watchman's sounds, I can't help but cover my head tightly, hoping I can sleep quietly. The truth is quite the opposite; covering my head only makes my eyes unable to see, but my ears are even more astute. The sound of the watchman seems to be just outside my bedroom window, even resounding beside my pillow.

The watchman is a short, old man with a pair of severe nearsighted eyes. I don't know when he took up this profession. And the townspeople have never valued this profession. He doesn't have a monthly fee for his watchman duties, nor does he have a watchtower to shelter him from the wind and rain. He lives alone in the earth god shrine. Every festival,

Page 16

like a beggar, he goes door to door to ask for a little reward money, and some seasonal foods: such as New Year's cakes, Dragon Boat Festival dumplings, and Mid-Autumn Festival mooncakes. At the end of the year, some wealthy families will generously give him some leftovers. He lives such a meager life.

This summer, the old man fell ill and didn't come out to do his rounds for a few days. It just so happened that there were two burglaries in the town during those few days. When the victims realized they had lost something and felt the pain, they suddenly paid attention to the watchman's profession, sending people to责骂 the old man for not doing his rounds because he was sick, and that he would have to compensate for the lost items. This was naturally just talk, or perhaps the person sent there added his own salt and sauce. But the next day, the old man really came out to do his rounds, even though he was still sick.

When cooling off in the summer heat, I saw him, like a toad, walking from the east end of town to the west end, a bamboo tube hanging in front of his chest, and a copper gong in his hand, striking the gong,du du dang dang. When he reached my door, he asked the people sitting there for a cup of tea. Because he was nearsighted, he casually called out "Madam, Grandma, I ask for a cup of tea to drink." He was as pitiable as a beggar.

I don't know who, let out a long sigh, and then someone began to ask him questions. Perhaps he was also tired, so he sat on the stone steps and recounted his life story. He said:

"...Watchman duties have been passed down from my grandfather's generation. It was during my grandfather's time that there was a major burglary in the town, and it was decided by everyone to cancel the monthly fee of one string of cash per household, only asking for a little reward money on festivals. This job has always been difficult, and at my age, I don't have any relatives. One son混s around in the temple grounds as a hooligan, and he doesn't even recognize me, his old man… Those short-lived thieves are also working against me; they stole things after I was sick for a few days…"

After drinking the tea, he continued on his way, striking the gong and clapper. That night, he seemed to be striking the gong with great vigor. When I woke up, I always heard him passing outside the wall. Once, I was even woken up by the sound of the gong.

But the next morning, someone found him lying under a cabbage tree on the east side of town, his face青 and white foam coming from his mouth, already unconscious. They carried him back to the earth god shrine, and he only regained consciousness, telling them sporadically that when he was doing his rounds to the east side of town, he saw someone leaning against the cabbage tree in the distance. He coughed and struck the gong even louder, but that person ignored him. When he rushed over, it felt like he had been struck by a palm, and he became unconscious.

So some people speculated that there were妖s on the ginkgo tree, and brought out some old stories to prove that the tree had been struck by lightning before. Others said that the old man was ill and had made it all up. In short, the night watchman died just like that.

For several months, no one continued the profession, although some people had suggested that each household should still pay a monthly fee to hire a night watchman. Unexpectedly, the old man's son, who混s around in the temple grounds as a hooligan, quietly returned to town. Without caring whether people agreed or not, he went to the earth god shrine to inherit his father's legacy – a bamboo tube, and a copper gong – and started doing his rounds, and he even knew how to sing: "Cold weather in the twelfth lunar month, be careful with fire!" or "Check the front door, prop up the back door." The folk songs remind people to be careful of fire and thieves.

It has been several months since I heard the sound of the gong, and now it sounds very uncomfortable, although many families welcome this diligent watchman. I really want to see that young man. Isn't it very free to be a hooligan? Isn't it a lucrative job to be a hooligan in the temple grounds? But he is willing to take over this profession that is not valued by others.

Now he is coming back from the east side of town, and when he passes outside my wall, he is singing the folk song "Be careful with fire!" Perhaps the wind is blowing outside?

God's Mercy Store 170

— Special

In Waller Town, Texas, USA, there is a store that is completely different from ordinary stores. Looking at its signboard is quite astonishing, which reads: "God's Mercy Store." The word "God" is written extra large. Any Christian passing by the store will surely notice these big characters. In front of the store, there is also a large wooden advertisement board, which reads:

"All goods in this store are sold at cost price, without any additional profit. Customers are welcome to make donations at their discretion in addition to the purchase price. The store will be most grateful."

Reading these few lines of advertisement, one can understand the nature of this store. It turns out that the items displayed in this store are sold to customers at the cost price, plus shipping and other expenses, without adding any additional profit. Customers may, if they wish, pay some reward fee in addition to the purchase price, no matter how much, it is up to them. If they don't pay a single penny in addition to the purchase price, they are treated the same. Some customers pay as much as 20% of the goods' price as a reward fee, while others buy at cost price without paying any extra amount. However, the store owner never frowns because of this, nor does he make things difficult. To those who pay a reward fee, he only expresses a simple thank you, without showing any special gratitude.

This store is located in a one-story house made of tin sheets and has a history of twenty-two years. When it first opened, it was very small, but now it has expanded into a large store with several entrances. The items sold include groceries, dry goods, hardware, meat, and various food items. There is also a retail gas station. Ranchers and farmers within forty or fifty miles come by car to support the store, so it is often crowded with customers. In times of economic recession, other stores have sluggish business, but this "God's Mercy Store" still has a thriving business.

The owner of this store is named Pei Weisi. He wears gray pants, a collarless shirt, with his sleeves rolled up, standing behind the iron railing in front of the counter. The hair on his forehead is very sparse, and he is almost sixty years old. His blue eyes and the wrinkles at the corners of his eyes give a very humorous and kind impression. He often talks and laughs with customers. Since he established this store, many neighbors and customers have rushed to enjoy this cheap opportunity. Many of them only buy things at cost and leave without paying any extra reward fee. One old customer once said to others: "Pei Weisi is willing to be a fool, but I won't be a fool. Over the years, I have bought things in his store, and I have never paid a penny more than the cost price." However, Pei Weisi still treats this penny-pinching economist the same as other customers and has never shown the slightest dissatisfaction in his words or expressions. One day, this person again purchased many items from the store. As per his old habit, he paid the cost price and loaded the goods onto his truck and left. But in less than a few minutes, he returned to the store, jumped off the carriage, ran into the store, and took out a twenty-dollar bill, handing it to the store owner, saying: "I can't always buy goods at cost price and not give the "God's Mercy Store" a little reward."

Speaking of the motive for Mr. Pei Weisi to open this store, there is a legend. Originally, Mr. Pei was a worker who knelt in the dust of cotton fields picking cotton flowers. He had not received a good education, nor did he have any connection with any church. Twenty-two years ago, while he was working in the field, he suddenly felt a surge of blood throughout his body and received a revelation from God, instructing him to start this kind of business to serve men, women, old, and young, that is, to serve God. It is said that even the name of the store was revealed by God. Mr. Pei once said to others: "I have never been a clerk in a store, nor have I ever thought of opening a store. I received a revelation from God, so I sold everything I owned and opened this store. I never thought about whether I could make a living from this, I only knew to follow God's command. This store has grown steadily. I use all the reward money I get in the store. This is not my wealth, nor is it my business. The bigger the store, the more I can serve." Judging from Mr. Pei's daily words and deeds, he seems very honest, treats people with courtesy, and does not like to exaggerate at all. Sometimes, newspaper reporters want to take his portrait and publish it in the newspaper, but he always refuses. In this way, it doesn't seem like he opened this store to falsely invoke God's name, to create novelty and gain false reputation. But that legend, we can only listen to it with a grain of salt.

Another feature of this store is that the partners in the store do not receive a salary. At the end of each month, Mr. Pei adds up the total amount of reward money paid by customers, and then Mr. Pei distributes it according to the size of each person's job, with the larger ones averaging about four percent. When this store first opened, the prices of goods were indeed much cheaper than other stores, but now many stores in the neighborhood have risen to compete, so the difference with other stores is not much anymore. However, the brand of "God's Mercy Store" has already been established, and most old customers are willing to support that old man Pei Weisi, so the business in his store is always more prosperous than others. Mr. Pei once talked about the various types of customers in the store: "From these people, you can discover many interesting things. There are a few people whose financial power could buy my store outright, but when they buy things, they never pay a penny more than the cost. There are quite a few ordinary people who are very generous, and the reward fees they pay often make me feel that it would be disrespectful to refuse and ashamed to accept."

A store like Pei Weisi's can be called a store with a clear conscience. Are the old clichés of "great bargain," "great sacrifice," and "honesty to all, no double pricing" that "our country" speaks of still worth considering?

Movies

Amateur Drama Actor Information "Thunderstorm" in Ye Lucy's Room 174

After the announcement of the third public performance program, rehearsals have been actively carried out in recent days, and the work is very intense. There were originally two rehearsal locations, one is the Ye Yu Drama Actor Association, and the other borrowed the address of the Drama Friendship Society. The three plays "Thunderstorm," "Stupid Pig," and "Demon of Desire" are rehearsed alternately day and night in these two places. Since the general meeting was convened a few days ago to determine the date of the public performance, the work has become even more intense. With three plays rehearsing at the same time, the location is particularly insufficient, so the play "Thunderstorm" has temporarily borrowed Ye Lucy and Zhao Dan's boudoir as a rehearsal location.

One Night of Absurdity 175

Cathay Screening

Ouyang Yuqian and Shen Xiling 176

In addition to adapting Tolstoy's "The Power of Darkness" into the Chinese-style "Demon of Desire" for amateur drama actors, Ouyang Yuqian also serves as the director of the play. In recent days, he has been adapting the script and rehearsing day and night, and the work is very hard. Shen Ye, the director of "Stupid Pig," also rushes to the amateur to rehearse the play (Song Yizhou takes over during the day), often not returning until 4 o'clock in the morning.

Publishing a Commemorative Calendar Card for the Public Performance 177

For this public performance, a commemorative calendar card is being prepared. One side is exquisitely printed with portraits of the actors, and the other side is a 1937 calendar and public school programs, etc., which will be distributed to the audience and students of major secondary schools. Printing is currently underway day and night.

Stars Shining on Huanlong Road 178

The two rehearsal locations and Zhao Dan's residence are all located on Huanlong Road in the French Concession. Because of the daily and nightly rehearsals, the footprints of many stars can often be seen on Huanlong Road. A small Russian restaurant has also been occupied by amateur drama actors. At lunchtime and dinner, it is often crowded and very lively, so Russian diners are also turned away.

A War Epic with a Price Tag of 2 Million Gold "The Charge of the Light Brigade" Will Be Released Soon 179

Since the release of "The Iron-Blooded General," the fame of Errol Flynn and Olivia de Havilland has instantly shone on the silver screen. Therefore, Warner Bros. has decided to spend another huge sum of 2 million gold yuan to produce "The Charge of The Light Brigade." The story is based on the famous work of the great British poet Lord Tennyson, writing about the joint forces of the Three Nations of Turkey, England, and France in the great war with Russia, when 600 elite British soldiers, under the pursuit of artillery fire from the left, right, and front, charged to the peak at the risk of death. The mood is tragic and enthusiastic, which is enough to the earth and weep the gods. The grandeur of its background and the brilliance of its performance are far beyond the reach of the two films "Battlefield Hero" and "The Iron-Blooded General," which depict love scenes, and the cruelty of the Indian massacre of the entire city is beyond the reach of films. The Great World Theater has been scheduled to publicly screen this film around the New Year.
